The Precursor to the Northeastern Army Entering the Pass 59

Shanxi Currency Experiencing a Bank Run

Shanxi Troops Gradually Withdrawing

Tianjin Correspondence: The attitude of the Northeast, which the whole country is watching, has now been revealed, and the situation is taking a sharp turn for the worse. Zhang Xueliang's ingenious telegram arrived in Beijing and Tianjin at 6 p.m. that day. The military authorities of Yan and Feng were quite embarrassed on the surface by this result, because the telegram directly addressed the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters and the National Government, which they had been praying for day and night. Shanxi Troops Withdrawing from Tianjin

to express their attitude. Initially, it was planned not to publish the telegram, but late at night, the publication censorship office telegraphed all newspapers, saying that the Northeastern telegram was not prohibited from being published. The newspapers then tried their best to find the original text of the ingenious telegram. On that day, only the "New Morning" and "Ta Kung Pao" in Beijing and Tianjin obtained the original text first and kept it secret as a rare commodity. Other newspapers were very anxious, and some newspapers even offered a price of ten yuan to copy the original text. The importance attached to the telegram by all parties can be seen from this. The ingenious telegram was sent from the Shenyang Telegraph Bureau at 2 p.m. on the 18th. At the same time, Yu Xuezhong, the commander of the Yushui Railway Protection, also immediately ordered mobilization. The first unit to depart was the 27th Brigade of Liu Naichang, followed by the 33rd Brigade (i.e., the Ma Tingfu Brigade). The two brigades, with a total of twelve trains of soldiers, departed at 3 p.m. and arrived at stations such as Shimen and Anshan on the east bank of the river that night. Subsequent units departed on the 19th. As of 8 p.m. on the 19th, more than twenty trains of soldiers had gathered east of Zhou and west of Qinhuangdao. The 4th train, which was supposed to depart from Shenyang for Beiping at 8:10 p.m. on the 18th, and the 8th train, which was supposed to depart from Shanhaiguan for Beiping at 5:30 a.m. on the 19th, both stopped selling tickets and were converted for military use. The 3rd and 7th trains, which were supposed to depart from Beiping from the 20th, were temporarily suspended due to a lack of vehicles. The mobilization of the Northeastern Army has been slow because, in order to avoid misunderstandings, it is planned to wait until the Shanxi troops have withdrawn before the Northeastern Army comes to fill the defense. Only a small number of Shanxi troops are stationed at stations such as Zhou, Guye, Kaiping, Tuozitou, Wuli, and Leizhuang, and they have already marched away on foot. The Northeastern Army is expected to arrive in Tangshan at noon on the 20th, in Tanggu in the evening, and in Tianjin on the morning of the 21st. However, there are still four regiments of Shanxi troops stationed between Tangshan and Tanggu, who cannot leave due to a lack of vehicles and have not received orders to leave. It has been found that the Shanxi troops on the Jinpu Railway began to withdraw ten days ago and are concentrated in the areas of Daming, Handan, Yuncheng, Cizhou, and Shijiazhuang. They will be completely withdrawn in three days. Feng Pengzhu, the commander of the 9th Army of the Shanxi side, took a special train to Dezhou at about 3 p.m. on the 19th to direct the retreat. The 101st train, which departed from Beiping at 8:20 p.m. on the 19th, was detained by the Shanxi troops when it passed Tangshan at 2:30 a.m. this morning (20th). It is feared that the transportation of troops between Beiping and Shenyang will be interrupted for a short time. In the past, five passenger trains ran between Beiping and Tianjin every day, but now it has been reduced to one. The Rehe Army also issued a mobilization order on the 19th. A battalion arrived in Tongzhou on the afternoon of the 20th to prepare to take over Beiping (Tongzhou is forty-five miles away from Beiping). Yuan Qingzeng, the commander of the Tianjin Garrison, suddenly fell ill, and the major affairs of the city are being handled by Mayor Cui Tingxian. Cui told reporters that he strongly supports Zhang Xueliang's ingenious telegram, saying that war and disasters only cause suffering to the people. Zhang's one word can transform peace and harmony, which is a blessing for the country and the people. When the Northeastern Army arrives in Tianjin, if they want to take over the municipal organs, he will respectfully hand them over and will never be reluctant. Before the Northeastern Army takes over the defense, the security of the city will be maintained by Zeng Yan'yi, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and there will be no accidents. All those with Shanxi colors are now showing signs of worry and are moving to the concessions. Since the 19th, bank runs have occurred at the Hebei Provincial Bank and the Shanxi Provincial Bank. The Hebei Bank issued approximately 150,000 yuan in fractional notes, and the Shanxi Bank issued a total of approximately 100,000 yuan in banknotes and fractional notes. Although there are no restrictions on redemption, merchants are taking the opportunity to profit by arbitrarily discounting notes from Taiyuan, which are no longer in circulation and have become almost worthless. In addition, there is one more thing to tell readers: After Xin Bosen took over the Tianjin Customs, the old customs officials, who have been in Tianjin for three months and still receive their salaries as before, are now preparing to return to the customs service after the Northeastern Army arrives in Tianjin, as the situation has changed. Also received news from the Transportation Community: The Shanxi troops between Zhou and Tangshan left this morning in a train of soldiers, heading to Xuanhua Prefecture on the Ping Sui Railway to temporarily garrison. Scattered small units of Shanxi troops are concentrating on foot in Fengrun, Lutai, and Tanggu. There are still about three battalions of Shanxi troops waiting for vehicles to retreat. At 9 a.m. this morning, Xu Congzhou, the chief of the General Affairs Department of the Beining Railway, spoke to Gao Jiyi, the director of the bureau, on a long-distance telephone call between Tianjin and Shenyang: (1) Please ask the Northeastern Army to cross the River and advance quickly; (2) Please ask the director to come to Tianjin quickly; (3) The Shanxi troops are seizing vehicles very urgently, and all eastbound trains today are temporarily suspended. Because Beiping and Tianjin are the locations of embassies and consulates, five or six passenger trains are temporarily running between them every morning and evening to maintain transportation and avoid criticism from foreigners. Fearing that the Shanxi troops will forcibly detain vehicles, we have asked British and French soldiers to provide armed protection. There will definitely be a new phenomenon after the Northeastern Army arrives. (September 12)

Reorganization Plan of the Fourth Route Army 60

Changsha Correspondence: He Jian, the commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, believes that the Fourth Route Army has been participating in anti-rebellion externally and suppressing bandits and eliminating communists internally for two years without rest. After the great war, it is necessary to reorganize it. In addition to submitting a request to the central government for the promotion of officials, the reorganization of all troops has also been decided and will be fully announced on the 21st to facilitate the reorganization with a military system. The main purpose of the reorganization is to change the former training of officers and to train lower-level soldiers, and to shift from ordinary military training to special forces military training to respond to the latest tactics and serve the party and the country. The reorganization plan is as follows: (1) The Fourth Route Army will add an army commander, and the 15th, 16th, and 19th Divisions will be designated as the 19th Army, with Liu Jianxu promoted to army commander. (2) The 15th Division will be reduced from three brigades and seven regiments to two brigades and six regiments. The division commander, Wei Suzhong, will be transferred to be a senior staff officer of the headquarters (he has gone to Wuhan). Wang Dongyuan, the brigade commander of the 45th Brigade of the division, will be promoted to division commander. Hou Pengfei and Wang Zhibin will be appointed as the brigade commanders of the 43rd and 45th Brigades of the division, respectively. The name of the 44th Brigade will be revoked. Each brigade will have three regiments, with an attached artillery and engineering battalion. (3) The 16th Division will be reorganized from three brigades and six regiments to two brigades and six regiments. The division commander, Luo Fanying, will be transferred to be a senior staff officer of the headquarters and will concurrently serve as the commander of the clearing of the countryside in Hunan Province. Peng Weiren, the brigade commander of the 48th Brigade of the division, will be promoted to division commander. Zhang Liangji will remain the brigade commander of the 46th Brigade. Liu Jiren will be promoted to brigade commander of the 48th Brigade. The name of the 47th Brigade will be revoked. Each brigade will have three regiments, with an attached artillery and engineering battalion. (4) The 19th Division will be merged from three brigades and seven regiments to three brigades and six regiments. The division commander, Liu Jianxu, will be promoted to army commander. Li Jue, the brigade commander of the 57th Brigade of the division, will be promoted to division commander. Duan Heng will remain the brigade commander of the 55th Brigade. Luo Shujia, the brigade commander of the 56th Brigade, will be appointed as the deputy division commander of the division. Deng Nanji will be promoted to brigade commander of the 56th Brigade. Tao Liu will be promoted to brigade commander of the 57th Brigade. Each brigade will have two regiments, with an attached artillery and engineering battalion (the above belongs to the 19th Army). (5) The New 31st Division will be reduced from three brigades and six regiments to two brigades and four regiments. Tao Guang will remain the division commander. Yan Zhongru and Chen Wo will be appointed as the brigade commanders of the First and Second Brigades, respectively. The name of the Third Brigade will be revoked. Zhou Xiwu, the brigade commander of the Third Brigade, will be transferred to be the deputy division commander of the division. Each brigade will have two regiments, with an attached artillery, engineering, and special battalion. (6) The 7th Independent Brigade will be reorganized from three regiments and three battalions to four regiments. Chen Guangzhong, the brigade commander, will concurrently serve as the commander of bandit suppression in eastern Hunan. (7) The Bandit Suppression Commander in western Hunan will be reduced from one brigade, two regiments, and four battalions to one brigade, two regiments, and two battalions. Dai Douyuan, the commander, was killed in action, and Dai Huiyuan will replace him as commander. Liu Yijing will be promoted to brigade commander of the First Brigade of the unit. (8) The First Garrison Army will be reorganized from one brigade, two regiments, and two battalions to two brigades and four regiments. Chen Quzhen, the commander, will concurrently serve as the brigade commander of the First Brigade. Chen Yunzhen will be promoted to brigade commander of the Second Brigade. (9) The Hunan Military Officers Training School will be renamed the Hunan Military Soldiers Training Office, with Hu Da appointed as the director and concurrently serving as the chief advisor of the headquarters. Liu Yinggu, the chief of staff of the 15th Division, will be transferred to be the chief of staff of the Fourth Route Army Headquarters. Guo Chiping, the original chief of staff of the headquarters, will be transferred to be the deputy division commander of the 16th Division to facilitate the implementation of the reorganization plan. (10) All of the above shall be completed by September 30 and reported in writing. (September 22)

Hu Ruoyu Reorganizes Qingdao's Defense 61

Qingdao Correspondence: Since taking office, Qingdao Mayor Hu Ruoyu has paid great attention to local security. He recently ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly guard against any negligence. As the winter defense is approaching, he specially discussed with Ling Xiao, the commander of the First Fleet of the Northeast, to reorganize the sea and land defense measures in Qingdao in order to prevent problems before they occur. It was decided that the navy would send warships to cooperate with the land police to be responsible for the coastal area and the Haixi District. The Public Security Bureau would be responsible for the Dongzhen, Sifang, Cangkou, and Licun areas in the city. The Marine Corps and the Security Team would be responsible for the area from Cangkou to Chengyang. After the above measures were agreed upon, the municipal government ordered the Public Security Bureau to order its subordinates to conduct thorough investigations of the household registration and check the inns to prevent criminals from hiding. More police officers should be sent to the docks and stations to carefully investigate. At the same time, a telegram was sent to Han Fuqu, the commander-in-chief of the First Army, to discuss defense issues. The original telegram roughly stated that the area east of Chengyang would still belong to the Northeast Marine Corps, but the area west of Ren Chengyang would be the responsibility of the First Army, and Han was requested to notify his subordinates not to carry weapons into Qingdao. Mayor Hu, because the defense of Qingdao has been reorganized, yesterday specially sent Cai Yuan, a member of the municipal government, on the Dalian Maru to Liaoning to meet Zhang Xueliang to report everything and ask for instructions. (September 23)

Guangzhou Municipal Government Protests the Results of the Shamian Passage Permit 62

French Consul Replies, Agreeing to Return the Embroidered Scarf Trade's Permit Fees

Guangzhou Correspondence: The recent collection of passage permits for Chinese people in the French Concession of Shamian has aroused opposition from Cantonese merchants in general. The first to report it was the Embroidered Scarf Trade, appealing for its cancellation. Subsequently, various merchants who regularly traded with foreign firms in Shamian also rose up to fight for it. The Embroidered Scarf Trade submitted a petition to the Municipal Government some days ago, requesting it to lodge a protest. After receiving the petition, the Municipal Government summoned four representatives of the Embroidered Scarf Trade, including Liu, on the 16th to inquire about the whole situation and collect various pieces of evidence. After the representatives of the Embroidered Scarf Trade reported the situation, they submitted the collected permits that had been extorted to the Municipal Government. The Municipal Government then drafted a letter of protest the next day (the 17th) and submitted it to the French Consulate in Shamian. The original letter roughly stated: "According to the representatives of the Embroidered Scarf Trade, Liu Shaobo, Cen Shaoquan, Li Yuheng, etc. (the Embroidered Scarf Trade's petition to the Municipal Government has been seen in previous reports, so it will be omitted), it is found that there is no precedent for this passage permit in previous years. Now, the French Concession Public Works Bureau has suddenly set up this harsh example to treat the Chinese. It seems that they are only concerned with the goods of foreign firms that have entered the warehouse or have been separated from the Chinese merchants, which is discriminatory and runs counter to the aim of maintaining friendly relations between China and France. In view of the above, in addition to separately submitting a letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government and the Guangdong Provincial Government for review, we hereby lodge a protest and attach a passage permit from the French Concession of Shamian. We hope that your consul will investigate and promptly cancel the aforementioned passage permit and return all the goods detained from the Chinese people. We also ask for a reply in order to maintain friendly relations." After this letter was delivered, the Municipal Government also sent Liang, the chief of the Third Section, to Shamian to negotiate with the French consul in person. At that time, the French consul also felt that the collection of passage permits from the Embroidered Scarf Trade was somewhat unreasonable and immediately agreed to order the French patrol house to return the passage permit fees collected from the Embroidered Scarf Trade, totaling HK$9. At the same time, he also drafted a letter in reply to the Municipal Government. The translated meaning of the letter, which was delivered at 5 p.m. on the 18th, roughly stated: "The collection of passage permit fees this time was due to a temporary misunderstanding. This consul also mentioned in a letter yesterday that the monthly tax of one yuan was decided by the Shamian French Concession at the administrative meeting in September 1929 for vendors, not for merchants delivering goods to Shamian. This consul is deeply grateful for the report from the Embroidered Scarf Trade this time. For the sake of fairness and impartiality, we are hereby returning the receipts sent yesterday, totaling nine sheets, and returning the collected HK$9 in full. Please forward them to the merchants concerned for verification and return a receipt to this office for verification. This consul has also ordered the French patrol house to only collect this tax from vendors in the future." Now, the Cantonese people generally believe that although the authorities of the French Concession have returned the permit fees paid by the Embroidered Scarf Trade, they still need to collect them from the hawkers, which is not a thorough cancellation. They hope that the authorities will send another letter to the French consul to abolish this example completely. (September 20)

Large Alliance of Songhua River Shipping Merchants 63

Joint Development to Avoid Profit Competition

Harbin Correspondence: The shipping industry on the Songhua, Heilongjiang, and Wusuli Rivers this year was very sluggish at the beginning of spring. Most of the regular liners lost money. The long-distance liners were still profitable at first, but recently, due to the large number of competitors and the mutual reduction of freight and ticket prices by the same industry, as well as the excessive number of ships opened, they have also become unprofitable. At present, there are more than sixty official ships of the Northeast Shipping Bureau, more than ten official ships of the Guangxin Official Bank, more than ten ships of the Dongxi Steamboat Account, and more than ten ships of the Fengtian Savings Society on the Songhua, Heilongjiang, and Wusuli Rivers. In addition, there are no less than one hundred ships operated by private individuals. The sailboats and small steamers are not included. Therefore, the total is more than four hundred ships. With so many ships, the competition for profits is becoming increasingly fierce, and the future of the shipping industry is quite worrying. Recently, the Shipping Association was reorganized and established to seek relief in order to avoid perishing together. Therefore, a general meeting was convened the day before yesterday. All the shipowners attended the meeting to discuss the results, and everyone agreed to the relief. It was decided that all Chinese merchant ships in the Songhua River should unite to form a large trust, with each ship as a share to jointly operate the business, and three major principles were established: (1) Freight rates will never be increased, but the prices will be unified; (2) Those who join the same industry will not have their personnel dismissed, but will be employed as appropriate; (3) The Shipowners' Congress will be in charge of everything and will not be subject to the control of any party. The business address will be in the Shipping Association, and no leaders will be appointed. The Shipowners' Congress will be the highest executive body. All ships that join the navigation will be subject to the association. The association will convene meetings to decide on matters and the chairman will make judgments. In addition to private individuals, the number of families that have joined includes Dongya, Guangxin, Fengtian Savings Society, Northeast Shipping Bureau, etc. There are still three or four families seeking opinions, and it is expected that they will also join. The general regulations and outline will be reviewed and approved as soon as Shen Honglie, the chairman of the Northeast Joint Shipping Bureau, arrives in Harbin. Shen has already sent a telegram saying that he will set off for Harbin in a few days. (September 20)

Investigation of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine 64

Approximately 210 Million Tons in Total

1 Million Yuan Needed to Restore It Next Year

Harbin Correspondence: Few people know the details of the Zhalainuoer Coal Mine's coal reserves. The new deputy mine director, Ding, recently returned from an investigation of the mining area. I met with him and, according to what he said, the Zha Mine has 220 million tons of coal. If 400,000 tons are mined each year, it can be mined for at least 120 years. However, there are some places that are difficult to mine, so the actual amount that can be mined is about 60 to 70 million tons. Coal deposits have also been discovered at Dalai Lake, more than 100 miles away from the Zha Mine, and the amount that can be mined is still included. In addition, oil mines were discovered 20 miles away from the Zha Mine. Its abundant reserves are unmatched by other mines in the eastern provinces. The coal seam in the mining area has a boat-shaped vein that is extremely long, extending 30 miles east to the Alkhonde station and west to Manzhouli, entering Russian territory and connecting to the "Zabaikalsky Krai" coal vein. Other north-south directions also extend very long. The coal seam is very uniform, averaging three zhang. Once a pit is excavated, the coal comes out of the two walls like a wall. Open-pit mining is the easiest, because the most difficult thing to obtain in open-pit mining is a continuous coal seam. In Western documents, taking from one pit is called "masu," but the Zha Mine has no masu disease. Once a pit is opened, it can be taken inexhaustibly. The Zha Mine also has four characteristics: (1) Convenient transportation: The mining area is on both sides of the Chinese Eastern Railway, and the railways north and south are all coalfields. The mined coal can be loaded and transported without any trouble. Even the Fushun Mine does not have this convenience; (2) Abundant reserves: Fushun can only be mined for 30 to 40 years at most. The reserves of the Zha Mine, according to what has already been discovered, are already greater; easy mining; the slope of the coal seam in the Zha Mine averages about 10 degrees, and its trend is extremely slow, making it easy for open-pit mining. The everywhere you dig can be mined. This is not available in other mines; (4) No faults: The coal in the Zha Mine averages three zhang thick, continuously without faults. Unlike the Fushun Coal Mine, which has faults intertwined, often when mining, soil and rock are found and the coal disappears. The results of this investigation have been submitted to the railway bureau, requesting an allocation of 40,000 yuan to start small-scale mining. There are currently more than 100 workers in the mining area, working on a small scale, half for coal for their own use and half for relief. This matter has been agreed upon by all parties beforehand, and it is expected that it will not be rejected. To restore the entire work of the Zha Mine, 1 million yuan is needed. This is still next year. In addition, the matter of restoring the Zha Mine, due to the efforts of the Chinese side, is not as persistent as before. The restoration next year may be possible. (September 20)

The Township Head Was Kidnapped But Fortunately Escaped Danger. Shen Renhe, the head of Xiaogang Township in the 10th District (Wuku) of this county, was kidnapped by bandits on the evening of the 18th, claiming thousand yuan ransom. boarded the bandit boat and sailed west. It is now known that after Shen was kidnapped, there were about ten people on the bandit boat. When they arrived at Jiejing, bandits landed ashore. The boat continued to move forward and arrived at Diao Bay tributary port. three or four bandits landed ashore and all left without returning. When they arrived at Pu Xiebang, which belongs to Fengjing, only four bandits were left to guard. Then, two bandits went ashore. things, there were still two bandits who suddenly fell asleep. Shen Renhe, the township head, thought it was time to escape danger. had arrived immediately tiptoed away from the boat and safely returned home.

They poured into the town and robbed from house to house, causing great losses. It is said that two people were kidnapped before leaving, and their whereabouts are still unknown.

Wuxi 69

Silk Factories Oppose Public Quantity Inspection: Since the Commodity Inspection Bureau under the Ministry of Industry and Commerce stationed in Shanghai recovered the International Raw Silk Inspection Institute and renamed it the Raw Silk Inspection Office, in order to correct the export of raw silk, it changed to the public quantity inspection system. Shanghai silk merchants, because of the losses and grade reduction caused by the implementation of public quantity, as well as the delay in loading ships, etc., had held a meeting to express their opposition. The Silk Factory Industry Association of this county also convened a temporary membership meeting at 3 p.m. yesterday. After deliberation, it was decided that all would oppose the public quantity inspection. If the goal of overturning it is not achieved, all will stop production to deal with it, and the representatives of each factory will sign to show their determination.

Qian Zhongliang, the Chief of the First District, Was Accused: Qian Zhongliang, the Chief of the First District of Xiyi, has worked hard in handling district affairs since taking office. Recently, however, Cheng Zhenqi and others, residents of the county, accused Chief Qian of encroaching on the private property of the Lingguan Temple on East Street. They submitted a report to the Civil Affairs Department listing the facts. After receiving the report, Director Hu ordered Magistrate Pan of this county to investigate and handle the matter.

Yam Boat Robbed in Broad Daylight: At about 1 p.m. yesterday, a yam boat belonging to Wang Junxiang of Yixing was moored near the stone pier near Xindu Bridge in the 17th District (Xin'an Township). Five robbers boarded the boat and robbed it, taking away 84 yuan of goods. After obtaining the loot, the five robbers went ashore and fled eastward.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Shuiqu Township: Feng Yunsheng, a resident of Xiaofeng Lane, north of Outang Bridge in the Fourth District (Kaiyuan Township) of Xiyi, is over fifty years old and comes from a well-off family. He is currently the deputy township head of Shuiqu Township in the district and has two children: a daughter who is seventeen years old and has not yet married, and a son named Yuequan who is fifteen years old. His father has hired a teacher to teach him at home. At about 1 a.m. the day before yesterday, ten bandits suddenly came, holding pistols and flashlights, etc., and speaking with a strong northern accent. Six bandits guarded the outside of the door, and four bandits climbed over the wall and entered. First, they tied up Feng Yunsheng and his wife with ropes, then they looted wildly and kidnapped Yun Sheng's son, Yuequan, out the door. At that time, Yuequan's sister saw the situation and stepped forward to stop him from leaving. The bandits were furious and hit her head with the butt of a gun, causing her skin to break and bleed. She had to let go. The bandits then dragged Yuequan out the door, fired a gun to show their power, and fled.

Hu Bin Plans to Build Leshan Garden: The lakeshore area of this county has beautiful scenery, such as Meiyuan, Yuantouzhu, and Liyuan, which have become famous scenic spots on the lake. Recently, Rong Zongjing and Desheng brothers, residents of the county, plan to invest 200,000 yuan to renovate and build a garden on Xiaojishan (opposite Yuantouzhu) in order to embellish the lake and mountain scenery. It is named "Xiaojishan Leshan Garden." It is expected that workers will be hired to actively build it after autumn.

Kunshan 71

Strict Investigation of the Case of Using Counterfeit Money: Since Zhu Pinxiang, the owner of Jixin Rice Shop outside the Shuixi Gate, used counterfeit Guangli Bank banknotes (some people had brought this banknote to the Rice Industry Association for sale some days ago, selling it for only four yuan per hundred yuan. Many rice shop colleagues bought it) to the villager Zhou Jingfu, the case was discovered. Suppression of Banditry in Dongxiang and Post-War Rehabilitation: The bandits in the four remaining districts of Dongxiang have been vigorously suppressed by the military and police, and they have now been defeated. The county government has ordered district offices to provide relief to displaced persons and restore the area to its original state within the shortest possible time. The highway has been repaired and traffic has resumed.

County Court Thoroughly Investigates Fraud and Illegal Detention Case: The County Court Procuratorate has charged Qin Naihan, the former judicial director of the county government, with colluding with bailiff Dai Bingyuan to commit fraud and illegally detain innocent people. Yangzhou 73

Bandit Robbery on the Hongda Steamer: Yang Gang, the son of the former Ganquan County Registrar Yang, was robbed on the 23rd while returning to Yangzhou from Jiangyin. The previous day, he boarded the Datong Company's Hongda steamer from Huojiaqiao. When the steamer arrived at Baweigang, a number of male and female bandits suddenly emerged from the dining room and robbed the purser's office of over 1,300 yuan in foreign currency. As they attempted to escape, a swift boat carrying members of the defense corps arrived to board the steamer and apprehend the bandits. A shootout ensued at the entrance of the dining room, resulting in the death of one bandit. One male and one female bandit were captured, while the remaining bandits escaped with the stolen money by jumping into the Yangtze River. The passengers were startled but fortunately suffered no losses.

Dispute Over Abandonment After Pre-Marital Pregnancy: Hu Jiren, a doctor residing at No. 10 North Xiaojie in the city, who already has a family, had a relationship with Wang Yueqiu, a 22-year-old woman living in the same residence, through the introduction of Hu's sister. This relationship has been ongoing for some time, and the two have privately pledged to be together forever. Now that the woman is six months pregnant and about to give birth, Hu planned to take her to the western countryside to rent a house for a private delivery. However, Hu's father discovered the plan and strictly forbade it. Hu then secretly gave the woman all of his house rental receipts as alimony. However, his father found out about this as well and insisted on refusing it. Hu then avoided meeting with the woman. Unable to resolve the situation, the woman went to Hu's residence alone yesterday (the 23rd) to reason with him. However, the Hu family kept the doors tightly closed, refusing her entry. The woman had no choice but to seek assistance from the Women's Association and reported the matter to the Second Sub-Precinct of the Public Security Bureau, requesting that Hu be punished. It is now reported that the precinct has summoned Hu's father and, along with the woman, has handed them over to the First Bureau for further processing.

Jiangyin 74

Arrest of Robbers and Shooting of Changshou Defense Corps: It has been reported that Qian Xiewen, Wang Xiaowen, and others from Qianjiawan wrote threatening letters to Qian Laowu, Qian Jiawei, Qian Zhikui, and Qian Hanlang, demanding 500 yuan from each. The head of the corps, upon receiving the report, ordered the corps members to arrest Qian Xiewen, Wang Xiaowen, and Zhao Heshang and send them to the county for interrogation. Furthermore, the residence of Zhao Shengfa at the Sigang Lock was robbed, and two suspected robbers, Zhang Guoxiang and others, were apprehended. However, the guards were careless and allowed them to escape. The Zhangxiang Defense Corps opened fire in pursuit, hitting the robbers in vital areas, endangering their lives. The head of the Seventh District, Wang, reported the matter to the county.

Seven Boat People Lose Their Lives: Xie Genlin, a man from Jiangbei, supported his family by operating a riverboat. He had a wife, Qian, and five children. In the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at 3:00 PM, the boat was moored at Huangtiangang Port when three men speaking with a Yancheng accent hired the boat to Tianxingqiao. When the boat reached Lubogang, the three men attempted to rob a eel boat but failed. When the boat reached Paozidang, the three men threw Xie Genlin into the Yangtze River, followed by his elderly father, wife, and all seven of his children. Genlin swam ashore and reported the incident to Cao Jinbiao of the Water Police First Squad's Patrol Boat No. 5, who then reported it to Shen Hualong, the captain of the Twentieth Detachment, to investigate the whereabouts of the robbers.

Nanjing 75

Regular Publication of the Continental News Agency: The Continental News Agency at No. 18 Madajia Bridge in the capital has been in preparation for a long time. It has now applied for registration with the Municipal Party Headquarters and has been instructed to proceed with the application. It has also filed records with the Garrison Headquarters and other agencies. It is scheduled to begin publishing on October 1st.

Gaoyou 76

Bandits Burn Smuggling Interdiction Gunboat: A smuggling interdiction gunboat stationed at Dianduo Village in the county was burned by bandits. The night before last, the gunboat was anchored at the Dragon King Temple pier in the village while on patrol. A bandit boat was approaching from the west. The interdiction soldiers immediately questioned the boat. The bandits opened fire. Realizing it was a bandit boat, the soldiers returned fire. The bandits, unable to withstand the attack, sounded several alarm whistles. Suddenly, a large force of bandits appeared from the rear to provide support. The soldiers, outnumbered and knowing they could not defend the gunboat, abandoned it and fled. The bandits then set the abandoned gunboat on fire in a fit of rage.

Devastating Fire in Shangliangshan Village: A fire in Xiaoliangshan Village in the county, the residence of Qian Zhaoyu, who runs a candle workshop, resulted in widespread damage. Zhaoyu's candles are sold widely. However, on the night of the 21st, at around 12:00 AM, a fire broke out due to carelessness in making candles. The fire spread rapidly, engulfing many homes. By the time the fire was extinguished the next day, only the Wang family's home remained. The rest of the village had been reduced to ashes. When the fire first broke out, Zhaoyu entered the house to rescue his granddaughter who was sleeping alone. However, he was trapped by the fire and perished in the flames, a truly tragic event.

Jingjiang 77

Investigation of Disaster by Hall Committee: Wan Mu of Land in Yu Daoxiang and Other Places in the Third District Suffering from Insect Pests, Previously Reported by the County Government to the Department of Civil Affairs and Department of Finance: Cai Tongmei, Inspector of the Sixth District of the Department of Finance, and Liao Yaoxian, Committee Member of the Department of Civil Affairs, arrived in Jingjiang on the 21st. However, the movements of Committee Member Liao were secretive, suggesting another mission.

Three Rebel Bandits Apprehended after Defection: Three rebel bandits, Chen Xigui, Chen Zhengfa, and Dong Xiaoquan, who defected with weapons and hid in Shanghai, attempted to return to Jingjiang on the Hongda steamer to instigate unrest. The Eighth District Defense Corps discovered their plan and, together with the Second Sub-Corps and the Smuggling Interdiction Battalion, boarded the steamer and captured them. A bandit named Chen Bibao resisted and was killed. When returning to the corps headquarters, they captured Mao Si, a former bandit who had defected but then fled, in the Third Dadao. They were handed over to the county on the 22nd. On the 23rd, County Magistrate Wang executed Chen Xigui, Chen Zhengfa, and Dong Xiaoquan.

Jiaxing 78

Robbery in Tanghui District: More than ten robbers armed with iron bars and flashlights broke into the home of Shen Youyuan in Beishenghang, Mingyang Village, Tanghui District, Jiaxing, late the other night, forcing their way through the door and ordering everyone to be silent. Shen Youyuan and his wife, Xu, were both tied up with ropes and severely beaten with iron bars, leaving them covered in bruises. The robbers then broke into the inner room and plundered at will, stealing rice, jewelry, and clothing, resulting in an estimated loss of about 300 yuan. Subsequently, the gang of robbers went to the home of Min Maotou in Liujiahang, Sizang Village, nearby, smashed the door with clubs, and ransacked the house, arbitrarily looting and beating Min Maotou on the head. After more than an hour, they left with their loot, which included gold and silver jewelry, totaling about 400 yuan.

Request for Re-Examination of Slaughter Surtax: The Jiaxing County Administrative Council previously resolved to levy a 40% surtax on slaughtering to fund public welfare and education. At that time, the fresh meat industry petitioned the province to instruct the county to exempt them from the increase, and representatives appointed by the industry petitioned the provincial government. However, no written exemption has been received after a long time. The County Chamber of Commerce again petitioned the provincial government yesterday to re-submit the case to the Administrative Council for reconsideration, proposing to slightly increase the surtax so that education could receive some additional funding without placing a significant burden on commerce.

Mingguang 79

Change of County Public Security Bureau Chief: Xu Zeliang, the director of the Public Security Bureau of Xuyi County, has been transferred to the province to fill a vacancy. Dong Zhangdong has been appointed as his replacement. Dong assumed his post at the bureau yesterday.

Bandits Attempt to Rob Shiba Town: Over a hundred bandits suddenly attacked Shiba Town in the county last night (the 20th). Fortunately, the townspeople defended it well, preventing a disaster. Subsequently, the bandits kidnapped more than ten people from nearby villages and fortresses and fled to Laojia Mountain.

Hefei 80

Elimination of Bandits in the Southwest and Execution of Their Leader: Zhang Huaikang, the bandit leader in the four counties of Hefei, Liu'an, Shouxian, and Shucheng, pretended to be organizing rural defense corps but secretly recruited outlaws and gathered disciples. The leaders of various bandit gangs in Hefei, Liu'an, Shouxian, and other counties, including Li Sihuatou, Guo Wuleizi, Xie Wudaizi, Chen Zikai, and Liang Chuankai, were all under his command. They were scattered throughout the area, engaging in robbery, rape, and kidnapping, all directed by Zhang. Recently, Zhang gathered hundreds of hardened bandits and entrenched themselves in the Sunjiaji area near Yejiawei in the southwestern countryside, plundering and forcibly seizing grain. The people reported this to the city. Song Shike, the commander of the Third District Bandit Suppression Command, personally led a large force to suppress them. County Magistrate Ye also led the county's self-defense forces to assist in the attack. Zhang stubbornly resisted, relying on the fortress. After a fierce battle lasting a full day and night, over sixty bandits were killed and the fortress was breached. Bandit leader Zhang was captured alive. Fifty-three kidnapped individuals were rescued, and over sixty rifles, seven shell guns, and two horses were seized. All the captured bandits were executed on the spot to appease the public. Commander Song escorted bandit leader Zhang back to the city on the evening of the 19th. On the 20th, he was tied up and executed at the Daguan area of the Garrison Command. In this battle, County Magistrate Ye also led his troops to capture over ten bandits. He returned to the city on the 20th and executed eight bandits at Huazigang and two bandits at Shangpai River. The remaining four bandits, Chen Xianfu, Chen Yide, and others, as well as a female hostage named Lu, were escorted back for separate interrogation and identification.

Hangzhou 81

Export of Over 30,000 Boxes of Honeybees: Since recent years, beekeeping in Zhejiang Province has developed rapidly, leading to an increasing export of honey. According to a recent survey, from January to August of this year, a total of 30,800 boxes of honeybees, valued at over 527,000 yuan, were transferred from Pingyao, Linping, Yuqian in Hangzhou, Tongxiang, Haiyan, Chongde in Jiaxing, and Changxing, Xiaoping, and Deqing in Huzhou to Moji in Japan for transport to various places.

High Court Assigns Two Judges on Transfer: The Zhejiang High Court has transferred Song Huachun, a judge from the Xiaoshan County Court, to serve as a candidate judge in the Hang County Local Court, filling the vacant position. Luo Dehui has been appointed to serve on a trial basis, and the Xiaoshan County Court and County Magistrate Yang have been instructed to transfer all pending civil litigation cases to Judge Luo for trial.

Pinghu 82

Revisiting the Old Case of Wang Mengxiong's Kidnapping of a Woman: The case of Wang Mengxiong of Zhapu forcibly kidnapping Ms. Zou Huiwen from Liujiatang in March has been repeatedly reported and investigated by the Zou family. The former County Magistrate Fang Li had issued an arrest warrant and the lawyer representing the Zou family had offered a reward for his capture. However, after more than half a year, the case remains unresolved. The newly appointed County Magistrate Shen is clearing up pending cases and yesterday dispatched bailiff Tang Zizhen to Zhapu with an arrest warrant to apprehend Wang Mengxiong and summon the plaintiff Zou Gu for questioning.

Founding of an Agricultural and Forestry Garden: Jiang Jingxiang of Zhapu founded the Oriental Cultivation Company on dozens of acres of land purchased in Lujiaqiao in the spring, suffering significant losses. Recently, Jiang raised funds again to purchase 80 acres of land in Haiyan to build a garden, hiring workers to cultivate it. He recently went to Shanghai to invite shareholders to hold a meeting. As a result, Jiang was sent to Ningbo to visit agricultural and forestry gardens as a reference, and to purchase a large number of Fenghua peach seedlings to bring back to Pinghu in preparation for the opening after the Mid-Autumn Festival.

Jiangbei District is also included. A plan is being worked on and will be submitted to the city government for approval soon.

Straw Hat Merchant Robbed in Yuyao: The home of Wang Yongtai, a straw hat merchant from Shenjiacaotou Village, Keyi Township, Yuyao, was robbed by more than ten bandits at around 9:00 PM on the 21st. The robbers broke into the house and stole 150 straw hats, clothing, jewelry, and other items, valued at over 500 yuan, as well as 60 yuan in cash.

Escaped Prisoners in Fenghua Gather and Rob: It has been previously reported that over sixty prisoners escaped from the Fenghua County Prison. It is reported that the village chiefs have notified the authorities to dispatch troops to apprehend them as soon as possible.

Shaoxing 84

Request for the Return of Firearms: During the years of the Republic of China 13 and 14, firearms used by the patrol teams in Shaoxing were purchased through local fundraising, totaling 160 Russian rifles. Later, the patrol team was ordered to be reorganized into a provincial team, and the firearms were borrowed but never returned. Now, due to the rampant banditry in the counties and townships under the county's jurisdiction, there is an urgent need for these firearms to organize local defense corps. Yesterday, the Local Defense Committee and the County Chamber of Commerce petitioned the province to request their return in order to strengthen their forces.

Series of Robberies in the Western Countryside: Fengshan Wharf in the western countryside of Shaoxing is an important thoroughfare for Tongtianle Township and villages above Xia Lvyuqiao. On the night of the 23rd, many bandits suddenly appeared and simultaneously robbed the homes of Yang Chunfang, Wang Nianzhu, Song Fuchu, Dai Chuanxin, and four other households, causing losses of over a thousand gold coins. The Detective Squad has dispatched personnel to investigate.

Bengbu 85

Arrest for Illegally Possessing Military Weapons: The joint military and police investigation office here recently received a tip that Gao Chuanjia, nicknamed "Little Overlord," who lives on Sanjing Street in this city, was suspected of illegally possessing military weapons. On the morning of the 21st, at around 6:00 AM, Deputy Officer Zhou and Investigator Yang led two armed soldiers and four police officers from the Third Precinct of the Public Security Bureau to secretly arrest Gao. Gao was apprehended on the spot, and over thirty counterfeit symbols with the words "Henan Anti-Rebel Army First Assault Team" written on them were seized. (Note: This team has long been disbanded.) However, no military weapons were found. Gao was taken to the office for interrogation. Gao confessed that he did have a pistol, which was registered in Huaiyuan, but he has now handed it over to someone else for safekeeping. However, he does not know where the person who is holding the gun is, so the gun cannot be found. Gao has now been bailed out, but because the gun has not been handed over, he is still being detained at the Investigation Office and has not been released.

Educational News Headlines

Zhejiang Province Educational Expenditure Budget for the Nineteenth Year 86

Recurrent Expenditure: 2,485,739 yuan

Temporary Expenditure: 350,529 yuan

The Zhejiang Province educational expenditure budget for the nineteenth year has been reviewed and compiled separately by the Department of Education and submitted to the Department of Finance for compilation and submission to the provincial government for approval. All items listed have been carefully reviewed by Director Chen in accordance with the current state of the provincial treasury, and efforts have been made to reduce expenditure. The total estimated expenditure for both recurrent and temporary items is slightly over 2,836,000 yuan. An approximate summary of the content is as follows:

Recurrent expenditure: 1,941,078 yuan in the previous year, 2,485,739 yuan in the current year, an increase of 544,661 yuan. This includes new projects for the current year, such as the Provincial Public Education Experiment School, subsidies for the Agricultural and Engineering Colleges of Zhejiang University to operate provincial senior high schools, the implementation of adult supplementary education, pilot compulsory education areas, the provincial rural normal school Xianghu area to implement compulsory education, teacher training communication research department, and the newly established vocational guidance center, as well as the establishment of two new provincial rural normal schools, etc. In addition, various subsidies such as subsidies for counties and cities to run public schools, public school awards, subsidies for private social education institutions, and the provincial education reserve fund are all new items for this year. The item for studying abroad has also increased significantly due to the impact of expensive gold and cheap silver. In addition, expenses for various schools have also increased slightly compared to the previous year due to the construction of school buildings and the development of students, but the amount is not very large.

Temporary expenses: 295,823 yuan in the previous year, 350,529 yuan in the current year, an increase of 54,706 yuan. Items such as the start-up expenses for the Provincial Public Education Experiment School, the start-up expenses for the newly established Provincial Rural Normal School, the cost of producing educational films, the cost of inspecting public education, and the temporary expenses for the printing house attached to the Provincial Library were not available in the previous year.

Letter from Jiangsu Primary and Secondary School Principals to Niu Yongjian

Three Key Requests to be Presented in Person by Representatives 87

Forty Jiangsu primary and secondary school principals, including Wang Maozu and Xie Jizeng, based on the resolution of the Middle and Upper School Principals' Conference, sent a letter to Director Niu of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Expenditure Management Office, suggesting three points regarding provincial education expenditures and requesting their adoption. They also publicly appointed Zhang Tong, Tao Xuan, Hu Shuyi, and Ma Ketan as representatives to deliver the letter to Director Niu in person so that they could present everything face-to-face. The original letter is transcribed below for your consideration, Director Tisheng: With respect, your support for provincial education expenditures has always been greatly appreciated. The principals and others believe that the financial difficulties of various schools have had a significant impact on the future of education. In particular, at the meeting on the 20th of this month in Zhenjiang, it was unanimously agreed that there were three requests that had to be presented to you: 1. Please ask the Jiangsu Education Expenditure Committee to thoroughly investigate the accounts of the Expenditure Management Office over the years. It has been found that the Jiangsu Education Expenditure Management Office has never published a formal final account report. Funds have been transferred and borrowed in a confusing and unclear manner. To rectify the Jiangsu Provincial Education Expenditure, the Jiangsu Expenditure Committee should be asked to thoroughly investigate all accounts of the Expenditure Management Office over the years to ensure accuracy and prevent abuse. 2. Please ask the Jiangsu Education Expenditure Committee to reorganize the Expenditure Management Office as soon as possible and relocate it to Zhenjiang. It has been found that the Jiangsu Education Expenditure Management Office is an institution affiliated with the province, and the collection and remittance of funds are closely related to the province. Zhenjiang is the location of the provincial capital, and the Expenditure Management Office should be located in Zhenjiang. Contacting various matters would also be more convenient. For the sake of convenience in collecting and remitting funds and contacting matters, the Jiangsu Education Expenditure Committee should be asked to reorganize the Expenditure Management Office as soon as possible and relocate it to Zhenjiang to facilitate convenience and conform to circumstances. 3. Request that the Expenditure Management Office release funds as soon as possible. It has been found that all provincial primary and secondary schools have been in session for many days, and there is still no definite news about the funds for July and August. At the beginning of the semester, the schools are burdened with debts from the previous semester, and the new semester is burdened with even more debts. Repairs and purchases all require funds, and the most urgent need is for the salaries of teachers and the expenses of normal school students. It is difficult for a skilled woman to cook without rice. This year, all counties in Jiangsu Province have had a good harvest, and the collection of education funds and taxes should not be difficult. The Expenditure Management Office should be asked to clear the funds for July and August before the end of September, and to release the funds for September before the middle of October to alleviate the immediate crisis and meet the needs. The above points are all crucial plans, and it is hoped that they will be adopted.

Jiangsu Compulsory Education Office Establishes a Teacher Introduction Department 88

Graduates of Correspondence Courses Have Priority for Introduction

The Jiangsu Provincial Preparatory Compulsory Education Joint Office has already established a local education monthly editorial department, a compulsory education survey and statistics department, a teacher training correspondence department, an education bureau public service entrusted agency department, and a popular education experimental area. Recently, in order to promote compulsory education, regulate the teacher resources of primary schools in various counties, and develop service opportunities for graduates of the office's teacher training correspondence department, a teacher introduction department has been added. It has also joined the Joint Association of Vocational Guidance Agencies initiated by the China Vocational Education Society. The department's articles of association are transcribed below: (1) All who need to apply to this teacher list and pending teacher list (two types); (2) Pending teachers should submit their graduation certificates and service certificates to the department for verification when making an appointment (must be registered when mailing); (3) The department may reveal special talents in newspapers and publications of the department from time to time for broader dissemination; (4) The department may provide appropriate supplements to teachers who need to continue their research on their knowledge; (5) The department may conduct appropriate tests or interviews with pending teachers at any time when necessary; (6) The department only assumes the obligation of introduction to both the hiring and applicant sides, and does not assume any responsibility after the contract is signed; (7) The teachers registered with the department are selected by the hiring agencies. In addition to opening a list for introduction, the agency will no longer participate in opinions on the right to take; (8) In addition to directly entrusting the department to introduce teachers, the department may also consult with the education bureaus of various counties to transfer the entrusted introduction; (9) Teacher registration is for a term of six months. If the term expires and there is no hiring, the registration should be re-entered immediately; (10) Applicants should promptly notify the department by letter of any changes to their contact information or cancellation of registration (must indicate the registration date for easy inspection); (11) Private schools and education circles that have not been registered are another contribution to the education circle.

Local News

Labor University Held School Affairs Meeting Yesterday 93

Resolution to Publish a Declaration and Prepare a Farewell Party

The National Labor University held a school affairs meeting in the school's conference room yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM. The meeting was attended by deans, department heads, professor representatives, and attending commissioners, totaling more than 30 people. Chairman Cheng Ganyun opened the meeting as scheduled. Liu Songgu, the representative of the president, reported that the school has been in difficult struggles for the past three years. The former president has not easily given up his responsibility because the budding labor education and the studies of more than a thousand poor young students may be shaken due to personal relationships. Now that the National Government has decided that university education should be handled by professionals, it should be followed in resignation. After this, it is only hoped that colleagues in the school will follow the spirit of struggle in the past and work hard to develop labor education. President Yi is also willing to use his qualifications as the founder to do his best to maintain the school. As for the financial issue, it is extremely difficult. President Yi is responsible for settling all matters handled during his tenure in order to maintain school affairs, and the salaries of teachers and staff for August and September will be issued immediately. After the report was completed, Professor Representatives Zhang Yousan, Yi Gengfu, Gong Xianming, Xiong Zirong, and others spoke successively, saying that President Yi had put in a lot of hard work in the three years of hard work at Labor University. Colleagues standing on the field of labor education should have a special expression to President Yi and should fight to the end to live up to the original intention of President Yi in founding this school. It was immediately resolved as follows: (1) Publish a declaration with the content: (A) Expressing admiration for President Yi's past achievements; (B) Hoping that the successor will have university education management experience, understand labor education, have the party's history and revolutionary spirit, and be able to inherit the old scale and expand it; (C) In the future, the school should continue to develop to meet the state's supreme intention of respecting labor education; (2) Hold a farewell party and designate Professor Gong Xianming and other five people as committee members to prepare for a memorial or memorial film and hold a farewell party and public banquet for the president and others on a regular basis; (3) Organize a temporary administrative committee to assist the school in carrying out school affairs before the new president arrives. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Chinese Expeditionary Football Team Re-Engages the Singapore Chinese United Team 97

Draw with Zero to Zero, First Time Chinese Win Two to One

(Singapore Correspondence, 13th) The Chinese Expeditionary Football Team, reorganized from the Dutch East Indies to help, played against the local Chinese United Team at Jalan Besar New Stadium on the afternoon of the 13th. Initially, the Chinese team came from the motherland to help and had a match with the local Chinese United Team, resulting in a one-goal victory, with a score of two to one, considered a successful embellishment to their trip. Unfortunately, they suffered a crushing defeat in the rematch with the Singapore United Team, losing three-zero. However, after the defeat, the team immediately led its troops to the Dutch East Indies, where the situation went quite smoothly. This time, they reorganized their forces and returned to help the association, intending to defeat the Singapore Chinese United Team again to boost their expeditionary reputation and wipe out the shame of the three-zero loss. Who knew that heaven has unpredictable winds, and man has unforeseen misfortunes? In the end, their desire became an illusion. Is it fate? I initially thought that the Chinese team could win two to one against the Singapore Chinese United Team. This time, after reorganizing their forces, their performance would definitely be better than before. Unexpectedly, the outcome of a fierce battle was a draw with zero to zero. However, was it due to the decline in the Chinese team's skills or the improvement in the Singapore Chinese United Team's skills? It was found that before reorganizing their forces, the Chinese team could defeat the Singapore Chinese United Team. After reorganizing their forces, they could not win. This shows that the team's skills have declined rather than improved. The Singapore Chinese United Team's skills have improved rather than declined. Not only that, when the team previously clashed with the Lok Wah Team, their team members were all strong and in good condition, resulting in a two-to-one defeat. However, in this battle, the team's important member, Mr. Ah Kow, was injured in his hand and faced the enemy while ill, resulting in a draw. Comparing the scores of zero to zero before and after shows that they have gone from a two-to-one defeat to a draw, while the opposing Chinese team has retreated directly from a two-to-one victory to a draw. Even the intelligent can distinguish which team's skills have improved. The strategic record of the ball battle on that day is as follows:

The weather during the ball battle was suitable with cloud cover, but the number of spectators was smaller than before due to the horse racing date and the past reputation of the Chinese team in Singapore. The referee on that day was a Westerner, Mr. Che Pengheng. The team members of both teams appeared normal during the ball battle. There was no score recorded in the first half. At the beginning of the second half, both teams were eager to attack, and the ball skills were impressive. Both sides had many opportunities to shoot, but the Chinese team's goalkeeper, Mr. Zhou Xianyan, and the Singapore Chinese team's goalkeeper, Mr. Ah Kow, showed their skills, "catching the ball" and "stopping the ball" like lively dragons and tigers, achieving unexpected victories. Also, although Mr. Li Guai Zu Huitang of the Chinese team had several dangerous shots, they were all stopped by Ah Kow. This kind of critical situation is not surprising to experienced players on the field, but the spectators on the field were given many false alarms. The Singapore team also had many opportunities to shoot, but they were all cleared by the opponent's Zhou Xianyan. In short, the ball game on that day can also be called a gathering of compatriots. The Chinese team came from the motherland and is a compatriot. The Singapore Chinese team is a group of overseas Chinese residing in Singapore. No matter what the ball game is, there is no success to be calculated. However, the Chinese team was lucky to defeat the overseas Chinese residing in Singapore in the first battle, and then draw in the rematch. If they compete with a different team, the results may be the same as this time. It is hoped that the athletes of the Chinese team will work hard in future matches with different teams, win glory for the overseas Chinese, and win honor for the team.

Shanghai Chinese Football Federation Charter 98

Full Meeting on October 6th, Fees Due on the Same Day

New members of the Shanghai Chinese Football Association who have been approved by the committee are required to pay membership and registration fees to the Association for Progress from today, and receive the constitution and registration form. Old members must pay the registration fee before October 6th to the association's secretariat in order to arrange the competition order and schedule. A general meeting will be held on October 6th at the Chinese Basketball Room. All new and old teams must send representatives to attend on time to discuss all progress matters. The constitution of this session is recorded on the left.

Shanghai Chinese Football Federation Charter 99

1. This association is sponsored by the China National Amateur Athletic Federation and is named the Shanghai Chinese Football Federation.

2. The purpose of this association is to promote amateur sports and improve football skills.

3. Any amateur sports organization in Shanghai that has submitted a formal request and has been approved by the committee of this association, and has paid the membership fee of ten yuan, will be a formal member.

4. At the beginning of each season, members who join the competition should obtain a registration form from this association, fill it out in detail, and submit it to the secretariat for registration within the specified date, along with the registration fee of five yuan.

5. Each team is limited to 24 registered players.

6. Unregistered players or members who have not paid the registration fee may not participate in the competition.

7. The number of team members may not be increased, decreased, or changed once registered.

8. The player certificates issued by this association are only suitable for use in the entrance of various competitions within this football federation.

9. This association has a committee to handle the administrative and all progress matters of the association.

10. The secretary of this association is concurrently held by the executive of the Association for Progress.

11. All competition referees are served by members of the Shanghai Chinese Athletic Referee Association.

12. All competitions are held at the China National Amateur Athletic Federation Stadium.

13. The competition rules are implemented in accordance with the Far Eastern Games football rules.

14. Members or players who violate the constitution of this association will be punished by the committee's judgment. The punishment methods are roughly divided into the following four items: (a) Warning (b) Fine (limited to ten yuan) (c) Suspension of membership or player's individual competition rights (d) Cancellation of membership or player's individual qualifications

15. Members are divided into five groups of "Chinese Football Association". The winner of each group is the championship team.

16. Each group competition adopts a single round-robin system. Except for the two groups of "Chinese", each of the remaining groups is divided into two divisions. After the weekly competition ends, the winners of the two divisions will compete in the final to determine the championship of that group (one final match).

17. The winning team in each competition gets two points, and the loser gets zero points. In case of a tie, both teams get one point. After the competition ends, the team with the most total points wins the championship of that group or the winner of that division. If two or more teams have the same total points, the championship of that group or the winner of that division is determined by the total number of goals scored in all competitions.

18. Players may not represent two teams in the same season.

19. If a member has a dispute, they should formally submit a protest to the secretariat within two days after the occurrence of the event for the committee to judge. All non-disputes must be accompanied by a deposit of five yuan. If the committee finds that the protest has sufficient reasons, the deposit will be returned; otherwise, it will be confiscated. The committee's decision is final and may not be protested.

20. If a team is not present within ten minutes of the specified time, it will be considered a forfeit. If both parties are not present, they will both be considered a forfeit. Forfeiting twice will result in the cancellation of their membership. They will not be allowed to rejoin the association in the next session without a solid guarantee approved by this association.

21. If a member withdraws or is disqualified midway, their existing competitions will also be cancelled and not counted.

22. If a team has to forfeit due to unavoidable circumstances, they should notify the opposing team and this association in formal writing 24 hours before the competition.

23. After each competition, each team should fill out the competition report form in detail and submit it to the secretariat for verification.

24. Each group championship team will be awarded a silver shield by this association.
