Local News 2

First and Second Mates of the Java Steamer Forcibly Assault a Chinese Female Teacher 216

Ms. Xiao Xinan is hired to go to Nanyang

She is alone on the ship and is humiliated by the Dutch

The whole incident is appalling

Overseas Chinese in the Dutch colony are outraged

The Java Steamer Company was established on September 17, 1903. At that time, there were only three ships sailing between Japan, China, and Java. Now, it has increased to eighteen ships. Every month, there are four round trips between Yicheng and Shanghai, four round trips between Surabaya and Shanghai that circle Makassar, and one trip from Celebes to Hong Kong via Borneo. The total number of trips between China and Nanyang is about 120 per year. In the past five years, no less than 120,000 overseas Chinese have taken this ship every year. The lifeline of the company is in the hands of the overseas Chinese. How should the company treat Chinese passengers with courtesy? However, recently, a case of rape of Ms. Xiao Xinan, a newly hired female teacher at an overseas Chinese school in Nanyang, occurred. The details of the incident are appalling. Overseas Chinese are under heavy pressure. Although they are doing their best to support this case, their strength may be insufficient. I sincerely hope that the diplomatic authorities and the people in the country will unite to help Ms. Xiao seek justice. The details of this incident are as follows:

Female teacher Xiao Xinan departed from Shanghai on August 14 on the Tjibadak. Ms. Xiao Xinan, a newly hired teacher at Peide School in Ambon Island, also took this ship to Ambon Island. Xiao is from Yixing, Jiangsu Province. She graduated from the No. 1 Women's Normal School in Jiangsu Province ten years ago. She is nearly thirty years old and unmarried. She is quite stable and has a talent for conversation. Peide School admired her reputation and sent several telegrams urging her to come. She finally agreed to be hired. Ambon Island is in the east of Celebes, and transportation is inconvenient, so it is quite difficult to hire additional teachers. Ms. Xiao's resolute departure this time shows her deep concern for education.

A crew member rapes a weak woman. Xiao, with her weak constitution, traveled alone in second class. She was very polite to the crew members on the ship. This is a characteristic of our country of etiquette. Who knew that it would be taken advantage of by the Western villains? The crew member rape case occurred on August 25, one day before the ship arrived in Makassar. After Ms. Xiao was raped, she immediately told the details of the incident to the overseas Chinese on the same ship, hoping to get help.

The ship's doctor diagnoses her with neurosis. Tao Yin, the Vice-Consul in Surabaya, Xiang Xiamin, the general manager of the Zhongnan Company, and Liu Jingwen, a famous philosopher, were on the ship. They all thought that this incident was bizarre and inhumane. They questioned the captain clearly. The captain then summoned the ship's doctor for examination, but the ship's doctor vaguely diagnosed Ms. Xiao with a nervous disorder. Although Ms. Xiao is thirty years old, she is still a virgin. She has been teaching for seven years and has been very successful. Now, the ship's doctor is calling her mentally ill, which clearly shows the Java Company's collusion and adultery. After arriving in Surabaya, Tao Yin told the newspaper about this incident, and the reporter used his flowery language to greatly distort the facts. For the past three or four days, Ms. Xiao has regarded this incident as related to the national honor and has specially told the details of the incident to her friends and made it public in the newspapers.

Overseas Chinese are very indignant. After learning about this incident, the various overseas Chinese organizations in Makassar were very indignant. On the first day of this month, more than ten representatives of various organizations accompanied Ms. Xiao to the consulate to request serious negotiations. On the second day, the Kuomintang branch held an emergency meeting. They all agreed that this incident was particularly important for the future relationship between overseas Chinese women. Ms. Xiao is educated and knowledgeable and dares to tell the world about her humiliation. There may be many others who have been humiliated but dare not speak out.

Organize the Xiao Case Support Association. On the evening of the third, more than 200 overseas Chinese from industry, commerce, and academia held a gathering and elected Jiang Yusheng, Shi Jiesheng, Ye Tianxia, Gu Yicen, and other gentlemen to prepare for the "Xiao Case Support Association" in order to thoroughly negotiate with the Java Company (javacbiajaQanlijnco) and achieve the final victory. On the evening of the fourth, another joint meeting was held, inviting the consul to be responsible for the negotiations.

Ms. Xiao's letter to a friend. Now, let's explore a letter from Ms. Xiao to a friend and transcribe it as follows: Mr. Koukou, I am very grateful for your care and concern during the trip. I was unfortunately attacked halfway. Because of my shyness, I didn't want to tell others about this trauma. Who knew that two Europeans would collude and act evilly, forcing me to the point of death. Although I have managed to avoid the insult, physical contact can still cause some changes. Our country has always valued chastity, and I am deeply resentful and painful for suffering this humiliation. What is the joy of being alive in the world? The thought of suicide is circling in my mind again. I am afraid of causing trouble on the ship, so I close the room tightly and sew clothes to pass the time. People come to harm me, and in the environment at that time, it was difficult to call for help. I don't cherish my life, but I am thinking of my elderly mother, how can I reassure her? I am just stealing a few days of life for this. I think you, as a compatriot of the motherland, will definitely be able to provide support. Xiao Xinan wrote in tears on August 30. The original text of the告僑胞 (gào qiáobāo - message to overseas Chinese) Ms. Xiao wrote a "Record of a Weak Woman's Lonely Journey and Encounter with Danger," which she told to the overseas Chinese. The original text is as follows: I have been serving the community for seven years, and I have been in four schools. I dare not boast about the faith and reluctance of the students and colleagues in each school. You can know it by exploring it in the country. However, because I have been to various places in Jiangsu Province, I feel like I am sitting in a well and watching the sky, and my knowledge is limited. This spring, a friend also had the same ambition, so I did not accept the persuasion of the old hall and family, and resolutely agreed to be hired by a certain school in Nanyang. When the departure date was approaching, my friend suddenly changed his mind, and it was difficult to find a replacement for a while, and the school sent a telegram eight times and my ship ticket had been purchased, so I could only travel alone. It is well-known that people from Jiangsu are timid. I was uneasy in the center of the sea route. On the evening of August 13, my friends in Shanghai sent me to the 芝巴德 (Zhībādé - Tjibadak) ship and asked them to introduce me to passengers who were traveling with me as a guarantee. I traveled happily through Xiamen and Hong Kong, and all my fears were forgotten. After the boat passed Hong Kong, the wind and waves gradually increased. Although I did not have a headache, I felt slightly nauseous. Except when I went to the dining hall, I fell on the head of the bed. On the 20th, I felt a little used to it and my spirits were as usual. Thinking that every inch of time is precious, I took out the silk material from the box and sewed clothes to avoid paying import taxes. I started learning to walk early in the morning. Because the trousers were not very elegant, I sewed them on the rattan couch in front of the window in the room. The first mate of the boat asked what I was doing. I showed him the trousers. He pointed and taught me to turn to the electric fan. I followed his words, but before I reached the goal, he entered the room to repair it, causing his hands to be covered with black oil. He took his clean white clothes and wiped it. I took the electric fan because I turned it bad, and he repaired it. I should have taken water for him to wash it, and then closed the wooden window. I still thought he was repairing the window for me. I walked forward and told him where it was broken. He immediately hugged me in his arms and asked me to love him. I replied that I already had a lover for two years and could not love him. Please forgive him. Before I finished speaking, he stretched his tongue into my mouth. I quickly turned my head, and he kissed my face and chest indiscriminately, wanting to achieve bad goals. I cried and shouted for help, but my room was far away at the stern of the boat, and there were no guests on the left, and the male guests on the right and opposite had all gone downstairs. In addition, the electric fan and the sound of the waves were loud, and outsiders could not hear it. I ran to the window and wanted to go out of the window. He immediately knelt down and apologized and left. I felt that he knew his mistake and forgave him to maintain his position. After that, I felt a swelling pain in my chest and knew that my body was injured. Sadness arose. I wanted to tell others that because of his judicial status, I could not get evidence at that time. He would definitely deny it and only attract laughter. Moreover, after the incident, it may be related to my future, so I can only turn into a frightened bird, tightly close the room to prevent ferocious beasts from invading. I sat in a sad city and cried for my unfortunate destiny. The next day, the deputy came to the window three times and knocked on the door. I resolutely refused his request. He even climbed to the window and jumped on the boat to show that he was going to harm me. I ignored him. He left. From then on, I became more and more timid. That night, I was about to tell Mr. Xiang Xiamin that the first mate and second mate came together. Seeing them in the dark was even more frightening. I knew that my life was at stake, so I went to the dining hall downstairs and wrote a letter of farewell to my family, crying as I wrote. Mr. Xiang also saw it. Not long after, the second mate came to my side with a flashlight. I put away the paper and pen to avoid his harm. He said, "You write Chinese letters, I don't read them for you." In fact, I knew that he did not understand Chinese, so what was there to be afraid of? However, I heard this and my fear was slightly reduced. On the afternoon of the 23rd, at about 3:00 PM, the first mate came to the window again and greeted me to open the door. I locked the door tightly as I did yesterday and was safe and sound. I just sewed clothes. Suddenly, a first mate stood down in the window hole. I ran to the door, but I was too anxious to open it and was caught. I was kissed and touched. I struggled to escape, causing the spittoon to fall and shouting loudly, but no one asked. Moreover, after I shouted loudly, he guarded my throat with one hand. I tried my best to escape to the rattan couch and prepared to kill him. My left hand touched the scissors and my right hand resisted his head and kissed and bit my body. But his eyes were on me and I measured my weakness. I could not hurt him and was killed by him instead. Blaming others, I did not dare to take this cruel action. Finally, I stood up and planned to escape to the window. He immediately knelt down and begged for mercy and left. From then on, I became more and more sad. After dinner, I asked about the political and legal rights of the Dutch territory. Mr. Lin, a fellow passenger, replied that the Dutch people in the boat were in the highest legal position and everything could be resolved by reasoning and did not need to be intense. This made me more suspicious of the separation of political and legal rights in the Dutch territory. The words I wanted to say were buried in my heart. Later, I reviewed Malay on the deck and saw the second mate holding a can of food and a flashlight in one hand and said to me, "You will be going to Makassar soon, and we will be leaving tomorrow. I will give you a can of things as a souvenir." I replied, "I am passing through Makassar, and I don't want your things." He walked around the deck and came again. I used the name of the first mate to repair the electric fan to harm me and did not get evidence to escape his guilt, so I took his things and asked him to write his name. He agreed. I pointed him to stand on the deck and guard him. I entered the room to take a pen. Unexpectedly, when I entered the door, he also entered the room and put the flashlight and canned goods on the high bed. He locked the door with one hand and held my head and neck with the other. After the door was locked, I saw him unbuttoning his trousers and taking out his penis and pushing me down on the bed. I told him that I would rather die tonight and would not be insulted by you. He still continued. I felt his hand pinching his pants and entering my lower body. I cried and shouted for help, but my voice could not reach outside. Helpless, I took half a bottle of seasickness medicine from the pillow and took it. He stopped when he saw me committing suicide. When he saw that I was having a drug reaction, I was dizzy, my stomach was twisted, and my throat was blocked and it was very uncomfortable. He took the opportunity to escape. I could only cry and be unfortunate to be born in this world and even more unfortunate to take this boat with few passengers and many rooms. The most inappropriate thing was that I was initially ashamed and afraid of death. Then, Consul Tao, Li, Xiang, and other gentlemen and Madam Li from Fujian knew about it. At that time, the medicine bottle fell on the head of the bed and the vomiting situation was seen by them. What face do I have to meet people after suffering this humiliation? I would rather die cleanly. Unexpectedly, the next morning, the effects of the drug subsided slightly and my mind was clearer. I felt that this matter was not only a personal humiliation, but also a matter of great importance to the national honor and especially to the overseas Chinese. Because there are many wives and daughters of overseas Chinese traveling by sea, I think overseas Chinese are more concerned about this matter, so I hereby announce it and hope that my compatriots at home and abroad will resonate and help me negotiate with the Java Company until the company actually expels the first and second mates on the 芝巴逹 (Zhībādá - Tjibadak) ship and compensates me for my personal reputation. If I die from poisoning, I am also willing to go to the underworld. Consul Tao was very responsible for handling this matter on the boat, and after Makassar, Consul Tao transferred it to Consul Wang because Ambon Island belongs to Makassar. The day I got off the boat, I wanted to announce it to the overseas Chinese to avoid misinformation. At three o'clock in the afternoon, I heard Consul Wang tell me that the compatriots here knew that it must be because of my misconduct that this happened. How secret and wrong! When people enter the deep mountains, fierce tigers come to bite them. Whose fault is it? The enlightened ones have their own public opinion. As for the reason why I have not dared to announce it many times, there are also reasons, which are described in the following: (1) I was sailing for the first time and did not know how many types of staff there were on the boat and what the duties of each staff member were. I only knew that the deputy was in charge of the judicial power on the boat. What are the methods for reporting and punishing them if they break the law? (2) I did not know the hearts of the overseas Chinese and the political and legal rights of the Dutch territory. (3) Knowing that the first and second mates had colluded to catch one person, there was still one person to avenge them, and I still had three days and nights of lonely sea voyage to go after I arrived, fearing that resentment would lead to danger. (4) The original school and family of my job strongly discouraged me from taking it. If I died halfway, how would I face them? (5) According to my observation, anyone who wants to do this must have two purposes: prevention and avoidance. Calling for help outside the room will definitely hurt my body, and calling for help in the room will definitely achieve the purpose. My room is isolated at the stern of the boat, and they must have explored the surrounding area when no one is around before coming. (6) The tea room on the boat had already seen it. Who would be willing to be a witness because of the bread problem? (7) There were only a dozen people in the second class above and below the boat after Hong Kong. Half of the people were upstairs, and there were forty rooms. There were few passengers and many rooms, so it was more difficult to call for help. Moreover, my room was at the stern of the boat, and the sound of the wind and waves was louder than in other places. Moreover, in addition to two or three people who spoke the same language, the rest did not even meet and nod. (8) I have a family economic burden and a certain school has been looking forward to it for a long time, especially since I have an old mother in the hall. If I die, she will definitely die in a hurry, and it is difficult to die. (9) The end of the negotiations requires me to resign and hire a lawyer myself. I don't have this economic power and it is difficult to fulfill my wish. (10) There is a group of people in the country who hold the principle of not caring about other people's business and a large part of the officials are afraid of trouble and bullying the weak, worrying that no one will help to avenge this humiliation after it is discovered. Yesterday, I read in the newspaper that people from all walks of life can speak out against injustice for me. Now, I have learned that the Dutch government governs the country by law and that legal rights are fair and will never be transferred by power and emotion. No other country can do this. Moreover, now that I have the apology letter from the Java Company, it cannot satisfy people, so I am telling the world about this matter in detail. Who is right and who is wrong is up to the public to decide. That is what I hope. Xiao Xinan cried in Makassar.

The Dutch overseas Chinese are indignant. At this time, the Xiao case has aroused the indignation of all the overseas Chinese in the Dutch East Indies. Various organizations in various ports have come out to discuss that it is not difficult to find a solution. However, the law-breaking staff on the 芝巴德 (Zhībādé - Tjibadak) ship are extremely bold and abominable. The captain's confusion and hearing is inherently the position he must take, but the ship's doctor does not care about humanity, does not examine the facts, and does not ask his conscience. He even erased everything with the four words "suffering from neurosis" and reversed right and wrong. The doctor's duty is originally for charitable undertakings, but the actions of this ship's doctor are extremely absurd. Commentators say that Mr. Xiao should immediately ask a world-famous doctor for a diagnosis and then file a lawsuit with the "Netherlands Government Doctor Examination Permit Office" so that the colluding and illegal doctors can be hidden and the future of humanity will be bright. The situation of future progress will be explored and announced again.

Guarantee Deposit Fraud 217

Impersonating Lawyer Jiang Yiping

As Many as Seventeen Victims

Unable to Fully Recover Guarantee Deposits

Shen Guofan and Gao Jingyi Both Detained

Recently, newspapers have carried advertisements for China Agricultural, Industrial, and Commercial Savings Company, stating that the company's business office is on Beijing Road and its preparatory office is located at 504 Carter Road. The founders are Shen Guofan from Ningbo, Gao Jingyi from Songjiang, and Gao's son, Xiao Zhang. Their legal advisor is listed as Lawyer Jiang Yiping, but Jiang has never accepted such an appointment. These people are using his name without Jiang's knowledge. However, with so many unemployed people in society these days, everyone is seeking employment.

Page 16

Seeing this advertisement, they believe that since there is a location, responsible people, and a famous lawyer as an advisor, there is no need to worry about being deceived. People such as Cao Wensheng, Yao Xuanyu, Chen Shanqi, Pan Nianci, Cai Keming, Gu Rusheng, Pan Zuoyi, and seventeen others successively registered and took the exam at the preparatory office. Gao Jingyi, posing as the chairman of the company's board of directors, determined the amount of guarantee deposit to be paid by the examinees according to the seniority of the position assigned. The minimum amount was fifty yuan, gradually increasing to two hundred yuan, eventually collecting more than two thousand yuan in cash. Receipts were issued in accordance with the names, stating that they would be notified by letter when the company officially started operations to come to work. Later, Cao and others waited outside for a long time without hearing any news, so they went to Jiang Yiping's law office to inquire. Jiang then learned that he had been used, and Cao and others realized they had been deceived. They went to the preparatory office and Beijing Road to visit Gao Jingyi and others to recover the money they had paid. However, these people had already fled. They had no choice but to complain in vain. Until 4 PM on the 17th of this month, Shen Guofan suddenly appeared on Nanjing Road and was met by Cao and others. Upon negotiation, Shen invited everyone to Room 1446, Yongxiang Lane, Xinzha Road to discuss. As a result, Shen handed over two passbooks with a total deposit of more than one thousand one hundred yuan. Cao and others then withdrew the money and distributed it according to the amount defrauded. For those who had been defrauded of one hundred yuan, they could only recover fifty-two yuan and two cents. Cao and others were still unwilling to suffer losses for no reason and insisted on full compensation. Because Shen could not comply, they reported it to the Xinzha Police Station, which sent detective Yang Xinzheng to arrest Shen and strictly investigate the whereabouts of Gao Jingyi. Then Gao was arrested and account books and forged share certificates were seized. Only Gao Xiao Zhang had already flown away. Yesterday morning, Shen and Gao were escorted to the Special District Court, where Judge Sun Yuan presided over the hearing. Only nine of the plaintiffs were present. According to Cao Wensheng's complaint, "I went to register after being introduced by a friend and was assigned as the director of the cashier department, paying a guarantee deposit of two hundred yuan. Later, because I waited for a long time without any news, I became suspicious and visited Lawyer Jiang, only to find out that I had been deceived." The other eight people, including Yao Xuan, also described their registration process. Shen admitted that he and the Gao father and son organized this agency to defraud guarantee deposits and claimed that he had paid five hundred yuan in shares. Gao Jingyi shirked responsibility. The court ordered the defendants to remain in custody and rescheduled the hearing for seven days later.

New Evidence in the Consort Mei Case 218

Consort Mei's Signed Receipt Discovered

Handwriting Comparison Shows High Similarity

Case to be Re-Debated

The case of prostitute Consort Mei, accused of conspiring with Hu Yongquan to defraud Zhao Guangzu of his prescription, has seen Hu escape to Hankou. The debate on Consort Mei's part was previously concluded, and she was ordered to pay one thousand yuan bail while awaiting sentencing, as reported in this newspaper. It has now come to light that Hu Yongquan, who is on the run, suddenly sent a letter to Zhao Guangzu a few days ago, attaching a receipt signed by Consort Mei. The letter stated that the prescription was mortgaged to someone else for four thousand yuan. At that time, Consort Mei took one thousand yuan and wrote a receipt, which is now being returned. Yesterday morning was the scheduled date for sentencing in this case. Consort Mei still appeared in court, while Zhao handed the letter and receipt to his representative lawyer, Lu Qi, to present to the court for inspection. Zhao stated that since this new evidence had been obtained, the debate must be reopened and requested a postponement of the public judgment. Judge Sun immediately compared the receipt with Consort Mei's handwriting and found the handwriting to be very similar. However, Consort Mei vehemently denied writing the receipt. Judge Sun decided to have the handwriting authenticated by an expert and ordered Consort Mei to pay three thousand yuan in bail and rescheduled the hearing.

Maid's Elopement Related to Dentist 221

Maid Sentenced to Two Months' Imprisonment

Dentist Fined Three Hundred Yuan

A Mr. Wang from Sichuan brought his family to Shanghai nine years ago and rented a house at 1008 Gongping Road. Wang's wife, Zhu, kept a maid named Hehua. She was just ten years old when she came from Sichuan to Shanghai and is now nineteen years old. A dentist from Fujian named Ren Li, who lived next door, often visited Wang's residence and became acquainted with Hehua. This year, Ren suddenly moved to 1975 Zhoujiazui Road, and Hehua also disappeared on the morning of July 23, stealing 150 yuan in cash, two fox furs, and many other clothes. Her master reported it to the police station and asked them to investigate. It has been two months now, and the whereabouts of the maid are still unknown. The day before yesterday afternoon, Wang and Zhu were out on business and unexpectedly met Hehua on Yuezhou Road. The maid saw the madam and wanted to avoid her, but she was pointed out and taken to the Huishan Police Station by the sentry post. According to Hehua's confession, after escaping from the Wang family, she first went to Ren Li's residence to ask him for help. Ren rented a room for her at 96 Yuezhou Road so that she could live there. The rent and food expenses cost a total of ten yuan per month, all provided by Ren Li. The stolen clothes, except for a part that is still at 96 Yuezhou Road, were deposited with Ren, including a fox fur coat and other clothes. The police head ordered detective Cao Xirong to first go to Hehua's hideout to seize dozens of stolen clothes, and then went to Ren Li's house to seize the fox fur and other clothes. Ren Li was arrested along with Hehua. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Special District Court. Hehua was charged with theft, and Ren Li was charged with receiving stolen goods. Judge Ge Zhiqin presided over the hearing. Wang and Zhu explained the maid's elopement after being seduced by Ren Li and hired lawyer Fan Gang to request an investigation. Hehua confessed that she had been abused by her master, so she took her own clothes and her master's discarded clothes and ran away, and had no relationship with Ren. Ren confessed that he rented a house for the maid to live in, but had no other relationship with her. Judge Ge verified the confessions and sentenced Hehua to two months' imprisonment for theft and Ren Li to a fine of three hundred yuan for receiving stolen goods. If he was unable to pay, he could be imprisoned for one day for every two yuan. The stolen goods were to be returned to the plaintiff.

Ye Xu Suffered Burns to Head and Face

Two Girls Rescued by Neighbors

Ye Xu, 27 years old, a resident of No. 14 Dunlili, Yokohama Bridge, North Sichuan Road, has two children, four and two years old. At noon yesterday, while Xu was cooking in the kitchen downstairs, the two children were playing happily in the room. After a while, the older child crawled into the pavilion room and started playing with fire. In an instant, the wall caught fire and the flames blazed up, spreading rapidly. Fortunately, the fire brigade arrived and worked hard to extinguish the fire for half an hour. A total of two houses were destroyed. When Xu heard the fire alarm, she panicked and wanted to save her two children. She rushed upstairs without regard for her own safety and charged into the burning house, suffering severe burns to her face. She was then taken to Tongren Hospital by ambulance for treatment. However, the two children had already been rescued by neighbors and were spared from disaster.

Li-Chen Wedding 237

Li Yushu, a native of Zhongshan, Guangdong, graduated from Queen's College, Hong Kong, and went to England to study at Oxford University, where he obtained a doctorate in literature. He has served as a postal official in the Shandong Postal Bureau, Director of the Ningbo Postal Bureau, Secretary-General of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, acting General Manager, Deputy Commander of the Fujian Salt Inspectorate, Inspector of the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance, and First-Class Clerk of the Purchasing Committee of the Ministry of Railways. Yesterday, he married Ms. Chen Sufang at his residence. In promoting the principle of thrifty marriage, all customs were abolished, and gifts from relatives and friends were declined. Many agencies, organizations, and relatives and friends came to congratulate him, and the scene was very lively. It is heard that Ms. Chen is from a prominent family in Guangdong and graduated from a women's college in Hankou. She is both talented and beautiful, a perfect match.

Martial Arts Novel "Ball Dragon" to be Published Soon 238

Zhang Chunfan, the famous novelist and owner of Shuliu Mountain House, previously wrote "Nine Tails," which was popular throughout the country and was regarded by social figures as a masterpiece of social realism. Little did they know that Zhang had a passion for martial arts since childhood and had devoted himself to research for three years, writing a martial arts novel called "Ball Dragon," which is tens of thousands of words long and fully expresses Zhang's talents. It is truly Zhang's greatest masterpiece in forty years and is far from being comparable to ordinary works on the market. The book will be published soon and will be a unique and dazzling addition to the literary world. All those who love to read martial arts novels can feast their eyes.

"Fulton's Magic Lessons" to be Published 239

"Fulton's Key to Magic," a famous French magic book, has now been obtained by Zou Dazhao, a student studying in France, at a high price. Zhou Shixun and Shen Hengxin have been asked to translate it into Chinese for publication in separate lessons. It is heard that the first lesson, "Male Entertainment" (i.e., Nie Gela's discourse on the destruction of women), has now been printed with extremely detailed illustrations. After reading it, one can perform according to the illustrations, which is very interesting. Fulton is the most famous magician in France, and his secret instructions for various magic props are very thorough and not found in ordinary magic books. This lesson is expected to be published by the end of this month. The entire book is printed on high-quality Daolin paper with a three-color cover and is sealed with wax paper, making it exceptionally elegant.

Zhang Danru, the director of the office, has been in office for more than half a year and has spared no effort in carrying out various projects. Mrs. Mao Kelun, director of the Shanghai Women and Children's Home, recently received a letter from a friend in South Manchuria stating that there was a woman named Shen Yuzhen from Suzhou, 17 years old, who had been abducted and sold into prostitution. Yuzhen did not want to live this life and had made several attempts to escape, but had always been found and brought back by the brothel. They requested assistance in rescuing her. After receiving the letter, Mrs. Mao handed it over to the Home for processing. The Home has reported it to the Public Security Bureau and copied the original letter as follows: We have received your letter requesting assistance in rescuing Shen Yuzhen, a woman who was abducted and sold into prostitution, along with the original letter from Mrs. Mao Kelun's friend. In addition to forwarding a letter to the Dalian Women and Children's Relief Branch to investigate and rescue her as soon as possible, we are sending you the original letter for your information. To the Shanghai Women and Children's Home, from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau.

Recent News from the Hongkou Plague Hospital 242

The Hongkou Plague Hospital has only been open for two months, but its medical services have been extremely busy and the results have been excellent. Although it was originally scheduled to close at the end of the month, due to the resurgence of cholera since the beginning of autumn, the hospital, in order to prevent the spread of infectious diseases and valuing human life, has decided to extend its operations until October 10th. If the epidemic persists, the hospital intends to continue providing medical care. Dr. Wu Lien-teh of the National Epidemic Prevention Bureau and the report from the Health Bureau’s Testing Institute stated that the first case of true cholera discovered in Shanghai on August 28th of this year was also a patient of this hospital, Xia Fugou, who has already recovered after treatment at the hospital. Today, Mr. Xia, in gratitude for the kindness of being given a new life, presented the hospital with a plaque inscribed with the words “Eradicate Plague and Pacify the People.” Yesterday, he, along with his family, personally visited the hospital to express his gratitude with Western music. We commend Hospital Director Zhu Jing’an, Shen Huachen, Chen Silan, Administration Directors Dong Gengsan, Tang Jingshou, and others for their efforts in raising funds to continue operating the hospital, as well as Medical Directors Lin Chunshan, Zhu Xiaofang, and Doctors Lin Xiongfei, Shi Yongqi, and others for their hard work day and night in providing medical care. It is also heard that the hospital is facing difficulties in maintaining its operations due to the economic downturn and difficulties in raising donations. It is hoped that charitable individuals will generously contribute to this worthy cause, as it would greatly benefit the poor and sick.

Public Notice from Xi, Inspector of Works, Maritime Customs Department: This Inspector of Works, having examined the Bai Mao Sha South Channel East Entrance Buoy within the jurisdiction of the Jianghai Customs Commissioner, has found that it will be moved. Details of the situation and positioning are listed below. The Bai Mao Sha South Channel East Entrance Buoy will be moved around October 9th of this year. No further notice will be given at the time of implementation. All other conditions of the buoy remain the same. The new location is south 8 degrees and 43/4 east (according to compass direction) from the Shi Dong Kou survey pile, at a distance of 2.3 nautical miles. All nautical charts No. 2 published by the Maritime Affairs Bureau should be corrected accordingly. This notice is hereby issued for compliance and notification to all vessels, who should pay close attention and remember the details to avoid oversight. Be sure not to forget or neglect this. This public notice is issued on September 20th of the 19th year of the Republic of China.

Haibei Port Sand Lightship Relocated; Azimuth 247

Removal of Liu Hai Sha Shoal Buoy

Public Notice from Xi, Inspector of Works, Maritime Customs Department: This Inspector of Works, having examined the Haibei Port Sand Lightship within the jurisdiction of the Zhenjiang Customs Commissioner, has found that its azimuth has been relocated, and the Liu Hai Sha Shoal Buoy has been removed. Details of the situation and positioning are listed below. The Haibei Port Sand Lightship will be moved from its original location around October 8th of this year, converted to oil, and renamed the Liu Hai Sha Lightship. All other conditions of the lightship remain the same. The new location is south 6 degrees west (according to compass direction) from the Liu Hai Sha survey stake, at a distance of 2.7 nautical miles. All upstream vessels must pass the lightship to the right (i.e., the lightship should be on the left of the upstream vessel). When the lightship is relocated, the Liu Hai Sha Shoal Buoy will be removed at the same time. All nautical charts No. 3 and No. 12 should be corrected accordingly. This notice is hereby issued for compliance and notification to all vessels, who should pay close attention and remember the details to avoid oversight. Be sure not to forget or neglect this. This public notice is issued on September 19th of the 19th year of the Republic of China.

Youth Corner

Impressions of a Trip North (5) 249

— Su Ling

(5) First Glimpse of Harbin

The sun rises from the snow-covered eastern mountains. The passengers in the carriage start to stir and become noisy. My heart also starts to pound. The end of this long journey is approaching.

“Harbin!” The train stops at this station. All the passengers on the train scramble to get off.

When I walked out of the carriage, the first thing I felt was the cold of the north. People were wearing very thick cotton overcoats with high, large fur collars turned up. They wore fur hats on their heads. Some Russian workers were wearing large, long fur boots. I was still in my southern clothing, especially my felt hat and the collar of my coat, which was not fur, did not cover my ears, and they felt particularly cold.

After shivering in the cold air for a few times, I hired a car and left the station for the Art College on XX Street.

I had known for a long time that Harbin was divided into Daoli and Daowai. Daoli was the Special District, and Daowai was Binjiang County. The Chinese Eastern Railway ran through the middle. The Art College was in Daowai.

The car drove on the streets of Harbin for four hours before finding the Art College. There was no sound inside. Had it moved? Or was it closed? I knew I was out of luck and had to ask the driver to take me to a hotel.

After settling my luggage, I went for a walk on the unfamiliar streets of Harbin. Because I had encountered so many unfortunate events, I had become accustomed to them. Although I was alone in the strange northern frontier, I did not have a single friend or relative. Now I had come alone. Yes, there were many dangers of being stranded ahead, but I was not afraid of them at all.

Oh, it is so embarrassing and dangerous to fall on the busy road! But I fell twice! The snow on the road had frozen and hardened. It was very difficult for people who were not used to doing sliding step dances or skating to walk.

Daoli in Harbin was completely Europeanized, and it was difficult to find Chinese people on the streets. I was walking alone on this unfamiliar street and fully felt the oppression of the foreign atmosphere. I heard people say that Harbin is the St. Petersburg of the East.

I spent three days like this. Lao Ding came and his first words were to blame me for staying in such a big hotel. But I didn’t know. I was brought here by the driver. Lao Ding said, “I redeemed you from the hotel.”

“I really didn’t expect you to come.”

“You asked me to come. But why is the Art College gone?”

“But the Academy of Art is waiting for you.”

New Atmosphere at the Law School 250

The Shanghai Law School in the 19th year of the Republic is clearly incomparable to what it was before. From the outside, the towering new school building will inevitably catch your eye as you pass Jiangwan Road. The school gate and the Great Hall are also under construction. The busy workers and the clanging of hammers can be seen and heard at any time. Let’s examine the contents in detail. The library is filled with books, as all the book fees paid by students each semester have been used to purchase books. Furthermore, Mr. Qian Xinzhi, Chairman of the Board, generously donated 2,000 yuan yesterday. The library is located on the third floor, and the reading room is particularly spacious and well-lit. The desks and chairs are all new and arranged in an orderly manner. The students are quiet when reading, and walking in feels like stepping into a chapel for worship. You can’t find a trace of noise. The seriousness of the coursework has not just started this semester. It has been strict since last semester. The principal, dean of studies, and all the staff of the academic affairs office strictly monitor the students during regular roll call and exams. The chief examiner professors occupy the most important seat. Not to mention this semester, there are several professors who are truly rare, such as Mr. Pan Dakui and Mr. Wang Qufei. The old professors, such as Mr. Dai Junliang and Mr. Zhang Yaozeng, Mr. Wang Fuyan, etc., are especially rare in this transitional era. The two female professors, Ms. Ying Zhangsu and Ms. Zhang Peifen, are admired by people from all walks of life for their knowledge, and their teaching methods are especially welcomed by students. Let’s look at the spiritual aspect. Starting with the professors, everyone is full of the vitality of spring. Everyone seems to have unlimited love and sincerity for each other. The male and female students also seem to have dispelled some of the barriers. This is all worth praising. In short, everything is constantly improving and striving for perfection.

The Future of Datong University 251

— You Pei

Time flies by quickly and never stops for even a moment. The rustling golden wind drives away the scorching sun and brings a beautiful sky with bright moon, indicating that autumn has arrived. This tells us that the summer vacation has passed and we should pack our books and review our old studies. Therefore, in recent months, schools have been busy with enrollment and registration, turning day and night upside down. This is especially true of the newly emerging Datong University in West Shanghai. The history and development of the school have been published in detail in this column and in various newspapers, so I will not repeat them here. The school has increased its student body by more than 700 students this semester, and the new school building has also been completed and moved on September 11. Previously, the former principal of the school, Mr. Ou Yuanhuai, once said, "I work from sunrise to midnight, and I cannot rest even in my dreams." This was certainly a few words of hard work and dedication revealed by Principal Ou when he was in difficult and arduous times. But even now, the school affairs are developing rapidly and the affairs are becoming more and more numerous. The teachers and students of the school are full of the spirit of struggle, sacrifice, cooperation, and construction. In order to preserve the glorious history of the past, they are still continuing to work hard as Principal Ou said. For example, the new student enrollment reception was organized by the student union in conjunction with the school affairs council, which appointed enthusiastic students such as Yang Shaozhi, Wang Jianmin, Xu Zexiang, and Zhao Yixue to take charge. Although several reception committee members have sacrificed their time and energy in the past few days, they have saved hundreds of new students from the pain of being unfamiliar with the place. This kind of effort is not insignificant. Although the matter is small, the school's spirit of mutual aid can be seen in a glimpse. It is now heard that the school has completed the registration procedures on the 17th and officially started classes on the 18th. As for the professors, such as Dr. Huang Jingsi and Dong Renjian, etc., are all well-known figures at home and abroad, and their works and experience are extremely rich, and the students have also expressed their satisfaction. But what is most worthy of our attention is that the principal of the school recently announced the future development direction of Datong University. In summary, he said, "In the future development direction, in terms of material construction, I think the most basic buildings of a university, in addition to classrooms and dormitories, should have independent buildings for science and libraries. And we sincerely hope that Datong University will complete the construction of the science museum and library within three to five years. In these years, we must actively purchase books and equipment. Once the most basic buildings and equipment are reached, we will raise a fund of five million yuan to stabilize the foundation of the school. As for psychological construction, it is even more important issue for the school. In the future, the psychological construction of our school can be divided into three points: First, the cultivation of a sound personality; second, the cultivation of true knowledge and practical skills; and third, the identification and cultivation of leading talents" (see the Datong University Sixth Anniversary Publication). In today's society, which is full of old-fashionedness and accumulated problems, it is not easy for Datong University to be unaffected and to be completely renewed. And the school authorities are showing the students with material construction and psychological construction, which is really a unique enthusiasm of educators.

Book Review

Traces of War 253

— Yang Shaozhi

Written by Wu Guangshao, published by Beixin Book Company

War is about sacrificing many lives and materials. War is indeed worthy of being cursed. However, seeing the Chinese nation suffering a great deal of hardship, with hardship dominating the entire Chinese nation, in this dying situation, are we still willing to be content with temporary ease, or are we willing to struggle for a while for permanent survival? If in a critical period, we still care about temporary ease and say that war is a sin, I think this is truly digging our own graves. Therefore, although war is not a good thing, for the sake of the nation's survival, for all internal and external wars for national independence and freedom, no matter how great the sacrifice, I think it is still necessary. Weighing the importance of the two, we naturally have to sacrifice some lives and materials in order to seek the permanent victory of national freedom and independence.

Recently, due to the results of the European War, people in various countries are tired of war, and this reaction has also arisen in literature and art, striving to advocate non-war. However, if we carefully analyze the core of this non-war argument, how is it? The imperialists' so-called non-war cannot avoid thinking that they are in a noble position. After all, it is their act of showing some compassion to say a word of non-war as a kind of gift to the weak nations. In fact, this is the true face of despising weak nations. If weak nations also say that they should be non-war, this is simply digging their own graves, directly expressing their weakness, and indirectly begging the imperialists for mercy. And this is simply a dream. If we want our own nation to survive permanently in the universe, the only way out is that we should strengthen ourselves and prepare to fight for national independence and freedom, so that we can have the possibility of permanent survival. Therefore, texts recording such tearful, inspiring, lamentable, and sighing traces of war have great value.

Traces of War is such a creation. He uses the power of literature and art to depict the progress of the National Revolutionary Army. He wants to use the power of literature and art to express the glory of sacrificing for the nation, so that they are eternally engraved in the hearts of the general public and eternally infused in the blood of the general public, so that they know that this kind of war should be commemorated and praised.

This book tells us that

"Lin City, which had been stubbornly resisting the enemy for a long time, did not see any traces of beast hooves in this hasty glimpse. The sparse smoke mostly came from thatched huts, showing a desolate and declining scene everywhere."

Let's look at the situation in Ling'er's home in the "After the Looting" chapter, where the remnants of the warlords who were defeated and plundered the people were so tragic!

"As if two wolves were dragging a lamb, they dragged Ling'er's mother out from under the bed. She struggled as much as she could, and shouted as much as she could, but to no avail. In the end, she was lying on her back under someone wearing gray clothes. Another person blocked her mouth with a handkerchief and tied her hands with leggings. She was subdued, and her feet were still kicking desperately. The vicious wolf pulled out a shiny刺刀 and stabbed her leg fiercely. She could not resist after all. After about an hour, they triumphantly took the bag and left."

We know that under this heartbreaking state, suffering the brutal ravages of the warlords, should we work hard for the people? Can we still endure it? Can we still be content with the moment? We naturally have to brace ourselves, raise the banner of light, and bravely go forward to eliminate the warlords. This kind of war to eliminate great harm for the people and to seek survival for the nation is naturally necessary, and naturally deserves to be recorded and publicized in literature and art.

This book has a total of ten creations, namely "Yali", "Kidnapping", "Drifting", "Badge", "After the Looting", "Belt", "Expedition", "Return", "Regroup", and "Visit to Yue". "Expedition", "Return", and "Regroup" are consistent and describe the scenes and feelings that the author witnessed when he participated in frontline work. "Yali" describes a promising young man who set off to participate in the front line. He knew that it was glorious to die for the nation, so he was happy to sacrifice. The other chapters can be said to be anecdotes of military life and the general situation of the suffering suffered by the people during the military period.

From the chapter "Yali", we can see the author's will and show a stronger willpower, and further recognize the glory of fighting for the party and the country.

"Why should a good man's bright blood flowers disappear in the embrace of men and women? Why not transplant them to the battlefield where he fights for the party and the country!"

This is probably the proper consciousness of the author of this book, so he participated in the most front-line work. In this chapter, he further attacks how incisive and precise the old ethics of the patriarchal society are. Look at what Yali said:

"I know, I deeply know that fame is a false embellishment, and face is a pretentious pile. I would rather be a traitor to the false morality than a sinner in real life."

This is such a brave and stirring statement. She finally broke through the dikes of etiquette and morality and obtained the ultimate happiness in life.

In addition, after reading this book, what makes me deeply sad is that there is such a passage in the chapter "Return":

"Scattered encounters with a few colleagues, they were all in a hurry to ask me about the news of their colleagues. From the extremely painful, extremely angry, and extremely hateful conversations of these colleagues, I know that the original group of beasts who were making trouble in Jinan and wanted to destroy our national revolution were plundering there, eating people there, and being irrationally rampant there."

Readers, we should still remember, right? What happened in Jinan on May 3 two years ago? New shame and old hatred surged into my heart. We should remember deeply. We should wake up greatly.

Secret Vow 254

— Shuhui

By Jin Guangmei, Era Youth, Issue 6

The commodification of literature has become a natural and accustomed practice in Chinese literary circles in recent years. Authors imitate each other without feeling shame, striving to emulate those who make fortunes through writing romance stories. Thus, triangular, quadrilateral, and polygonal relationships are depicted in a chaotic mess, with characters addressing each other in intimate terms, acting secretively and furtively. The more sexual matters are described, the more they cater to the readers' psychology, anticipating high sales. Bookstore owners are happy to invest large sums to purchase such works. Consequently, a continuous stream of romance writers has emerged in recent years, creating things that are disgusting. Writers are happy to write it, bookstore owners are happy to buy it, and readers are happy to read it, but they are also being anesthetized without realizing it. Although this type of work and writer continue to be produced, another group of people who consider themselves to be part of the times believe that these are products of the past, outdated people who should no longer be serving as loudspeakers for the bourgeoisie and petit bourgeoisie, playing the love games of young masters and young ladies. As a result, literature that shouts poverty and hunger, slogans, and stickers has emerged, filling the market. Proletarian literature is a fashionable import, and who doesn't love fashion? Who wants to be left behind? Even old men with beards are starting to bang on broken gongs. In this situation, authors strive to create, bookstore owners are willing to collect, and readers rush to read. In short, the commodification of literature is a minor issue; the impact on society is nothing more than corruption and degradation.

Most lovers of literature are young people who are easily influenced. Young people are the inheritors of the country and the nation. If such corrupting and degrading ideas are instilled in young people, what can we expect for the future? Chinese literary works should reject and correct all past misconceptions, actively establishing a central ideology that motivates young people to strive for the nation and the country, preventing them from wandering astray. Such works are what we need now.

Yesterday, I sent my younger sister to school in Shanghai and bought the newly published sixth issue of "Era Youth" at a newsstand. Its content was surprisingly rich. In addition to theoretical articles, the most unforgettable piece after reading was Jin Guangmei's short story "Secret Vow."

"Secret Vow" depicts the humiliation of Chinese people in foreign films. The author uses concise language to write about profound and moving scenes, making readers feel as if they are there, watching the insulting portrayals of Chinese people unfold on the screen in a movie theater. The general plot is as follows: A very wealthy couple, who are usually arrogant and only care about their own interests, never think about their nation. Later, they see a foreign film depicting various shameful scenes of Shanghai insulting the Chinese people. They are slightly moved. As the film becomes more intense and bizarre, they become more tense and embarrassed. As a result, they become more aware. They cannot bear the pressure in the theater and finally flee home. They spend a sleepless night in remorse and then secretly vow, "From now on, we are willing to sacrifice and dedicate ourselves to our Chinese nation."

The author expresses that the interests, honor, and disgrace of the nation are closely related to all people, regardless of their poverty, intelligence, or foolishness. The disgrace of some is the disgrace of the entire nation, prompting the awakening of national consciousness. The author uses economical writing to encompass a wide range of facts, such as the opening:

"Ronggui, drive the car back and come back in two hours."

What economical writing! From these two sentences, one can infer how rich the Zhang family is, thus determining that the author is skilled at writing short stories. At the same time, the author's imagination is also very rich. The depiction of the scenes on the screen is very detailed without being tedious. The author describes how Chinese people in foreign countries are impolite, unhygienic, and urinate everywhere, coincidentally meeting a young and beautiful girl. This girl is naturally angry and resentful, but the Chinese gentleman not only feels no shame but also expresses a triumphant victory. Such writing is so profound. Also, "Those ladies in high heels were slipping on Chinese people's spit," "Hands full of Chinese people's spit," "Gentlemen in wide robes and large sleeves with eight-patterned long coats, square patches, red-topped hats with peacock feathers, hanging court beads, and high-soled powder boots, socializing with humble and subservient gestures. The ladies with bound feet walking with the support of walls, sleeping in opium dens accompanied by gentlemen smoking opium," "Chinese funerals with road-opening gods, ghost fighters, lion, deer, camel, elephant, Gongbu A-zi cards, twelve flower gods, eight immortals, and figures, ten-thousand-people umbrellas, merit boxes, Taoist sheng flutes, Buddhist chimes, nuns' wooden fish, gongs and drums, flags, and military bands—everything is available." It is written in great detail.

The author's portrayal of the protagonist's psychology is also particularly subtle. The most tense moment is when the screen shows more bizarre insults to Chinese people, and the foreigners laugh more happily. The Zhang couple becomes increasingly awkward and embarrassed, their faces turning blue, red, and gray, as if they cannot survive the day. Even the candy boy who walks in front of them has no mind to pay attention to them, only the tide in their hearts is constantly rising and falling.

"Although I have a beautiful wife, a tall Western-style house, abundant food and clothing, a new car, and considerate servants, I don't care about political affairs. Fortunately, my job is in the concession, my address is in the concession. I can do my job as a bank manager. What does international status or semi-colonial status have to do with me? What does it matter to me whether the nation is oppressed or not? But now, this screen has made me realize, deeply realize, that I see our nation being insulted, bullied, persecuted, and ridiculed."

Originally, Mr. Zhang thought of himself as being extremely individualistic, but now he is fully aware. Although the insults on the screen are not directed at him, he cannot stand aside from this shame. He thoroughly understands that the nation is a whole, and he is naturally a member of the Chinese nation. As a result, he cannot sleep that night, and the two decide to make a secret vow to each other.

Although the material in this story is inevitably influenced by the Hong Shen "Fear Not Death" case, the author further depicts such a sensational case of foreigners insulting several of our people into a novel, making the people of the country pay more attention to it, which is really commendable. This is truly grasping the work of the times. In the past revolutionary processes, how many things were worth recording, but unfortunately, no writer noticed this and grasped it. What a pity! I hope that future writers will do more work that guides life and write less disgusting things that are supposed to be interesting.

Page 20

Caoye Weekly 255

— Nanxin

Volume 3, Issues 6 and 7

In the realm of purely literary small publications, Caoye Weekly stands as the most exquisite bloom. This flower undoubtedly blossoms more alluringly, captivating the hearts of many. Its fragrance permeates throughout the Chinese literary garden, effectively transcending its namesake status of a desolate "Caoye" (wilderness). Particularly noteworthy and heartening is its unwavering central consciousness in both writing and thought, with each poem or prose piece infused with a rich sense of nationalism. Given that each writer possesses their distinct style, we, the readers, find it devoid of monotony, which serves as an elevation. Lately, the publication has further solidified its battle lines, with the sixth issue commencing with a poem-formatted "Message to Readers," exhibiting a steadfast commitment to nationalist literature that is truly admirable. A section is extracted below:

We possess an indomitable will,

We possess heads forged of iron and stone,

Fear not external alienation and slander,

Even less do we fear all difficulties and setbacks.

They nakedly expressed the attitude of their entire collective. They are performing in the form of a whole collectivist doctrine. The standard has invisibly penetrated the correct central consciousness of nationalism, and whether working on literature or other academics, in addition to having the correct central ideology, it is also necessary to have the determination to persevere to the end. The so-called external "storms" need not be taken into account, as long as one's own line is strict and solidarity is achieved, which is to increase the infinite power of progress. These are clearly told to us in this "Message to Readers" poem.

In the seventh issue, two articles are worthy of attention. One is a poem by Mao Mingdao named "Before the Tomb of a Warrior," earnestly eulogizing with utmost majesty, such as:

Before the tomb, small wooden plaques stand in a row, inscribed with "The Tomb of a Warrior Who Sacrificed for the Chinese Nation." After such a long period of wind and rain,

The handwriting is not blurred at all,

Not blurred at all.

Who does not remember that you are warriors who sacrificed for the country?

Warriors, you are all eager to fight for the freedom of the Chinese nation.

Only when the banner of revolution was raised to fight for the nation did we know that you sacrificed your lives.

Your spirit is eternally immortal, and your historical achievements will last forever.

Now, your tombstones stand tall, and many brothers who love their country have rushed to

The front of your tombstones.

In our so-called semi-colonial China, there are indeed many warriors who have fought and sacrificed for the Chinese nation who deserve ardent commemoration. Moreover, their great spirit and deeds can serve as a model for future generations to be brave, to rise up with heroic determination, and to advance forward. Such a narrative poem with profound significance is very much needed in the current Chinese literary scene. The author, Mao Jun, was able to find poetic material in this kind of historical fact, and the emotions are unusually warm and intense. The boldness of the words and the magnificence of the tone are all expressed in this poem. The last section is especially worthy of repeated chanting:

Listen to the sounds of the front line,

Listen to the bugle call on the horse's back,

Warriors hold high the revolutionary banner and move forward,

Igniting the flame of glory for the nation,

Rushing through the strongholds defended by imperialism,

Friends, let us sing loudly,

"Victory to the Chinese nation,

Warriors shout triumphant return!"

Here, there are not only descriptions of various forms on the battlefield, but also the mission that the warriors should shoulder to move forward, and finally, a powerful encouragement to the inevitable realization of what is hoped for. It is not easy to express such a complex connotation in a lively way in the form of poetry. Secondly, the short essay "Warriors, Recognize Our Responsibilities" by Wang Tiehua is also worthy of recommendation as a rare masterpiece.

The author's attitude is very serious. He uses profound insights to judge that all Chinese contemporary youths should quickly take on major missions and future goals. At the same time, he cites many historical facts from all over the world about "dying for the motherland" that are faithful to nationalist literature as the basis for "Warriors, Recognize Our Responsibilities." The emergence of nationalist literature is by no means empty or unsubstantial. It has its own historical background and realistic environment. In China, the profound theory of nationalist literature already has a solid foundation, and it is bound to emerge in the literary world. Therefore, the author once said very thoroughly, "The beginning of this great work is the establishment of nationalist literature. It is necessary to first give a painful criticism to the confused and mixed thoughts of young people, and then to give a sobering warning to the people wandering in the difficult times. In fact, historical facts tell us that we must fulfill this responsibility." This is an undeniable fact. In the last paragraph, the author writes even more powerfully: "Dear warriors, recognize our great responsibilities. Great responsibilities have been entrusted to us since history, and it is time for us to shoulder the glory of the Chinese nation for five thousand years, to stand up with weapons and begin to fulfill our responsibilities. Sweep away the evil mist, destroy the viciousness, and get rid of all tools of aiding abuse. This is the current responsibility of the warriors who fight for the nation." We, the readers of this publication, should pay close attention to this sharp short essay.

Manuscript Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Reviews 256

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the review. However, frivolous books and newspapers will not be reviewed.

Shanghai Market

Market News 257

Sincere Company announced that its fourth floor displays a large number of velvet curtains, serge curtains, velvet carpets, travel reflective photography lenses, and family movie projectors and educational films. The goods are excellent and the prices are low, so people from all walks of life go to buy them enthusiastically, it is said.

Tongchuntang, newly opened north of the Old Zha Bridge, announced that its ginseng, bird's nest, and traditional Chinese medicine shop opened on the 24th. Customers from far and near flocked to the store, and the business was extremely crowded. The medicinal wine, which was sold at half price, was in such high demand that they were unable to handle it. The secret monkey jujube powder, ginseng regenerating pills, and ginseng velvet white phoenix pills that were sold were particularly popular. The store's goods are of high quality and the prices are low, and it has long been trusted by customers, it is said.

Tongchang Motor Shop on Nanjing Road announced that its store will hold a special sale starting on September 10th. All kinds of motorcycles, bicycles, cargo tricycles, women's cars, children's cars, and spare parts are all specially discounted. Business has been exceptionally prosperous in recent days. It is learned that Tongchang Flying Wheel bicycles are only sold for $67.50 each, and 1930 Three Guns cars are sold for $120 each. All parts are even cheaper. Eagle brand rolling bells are only sold for $0.70 each, multi-purpose oil is $0.30 per bottle, copper polish is $0.20 per bottle, and Peiwen hand-pressed horns are $1.65 each, it is said.

Lao Tianyuan Copper and Tin Shop announced that its store has been established in the Dong Street inside Xiaodongmen, Shanghai, for more than 100 years. It transports famous copper and tin from various provinces to supervise the construction of different basins, furnaces, dowries, and Beijing-Suzhou instruments. The prices are low and the quality is good, and it is famous at home and abroad. Due to the daily development of business, a first branch was specially added opposite the makeup industry association on the north side of Zhonghua Road and scheduled to open on September 28th of the Gregorian calendar. Both the main and branch stores will be reduced in price for 30 days at the same time, it is said.

Yanhua Restaurant, opposite the Dan Gui First Stage on Fourth Horse Road, announced that its restaurant's various Cantonese-style preserved meats have always been famous. It was the first to produce duck liver sausage, which has been manufactured for more than 20 years and has the deepest experience. Therefore, the taste is suitable for people from all provinces, so the annual sales have been increasing. Now, we have received letters from all walks of life urging us to manufacture it early. In order to repay the kindness of all parties, the restaurant specially consulted with the preserved meat technicians and asked them to manufacture it earlier. It has already been made yesterday and has been greatly improved. The taste is more excellent than last year. All the ingredients are selected from high-quality foods, and the taste is very different from other stores. They are also decorated with exquisite paper boxes, and gifts to relatives and friends are all satisfactory. They are used for side dishes and hospitality at home, and they are the supreme treasure, it is said.

Qingyise Guangzhou Food Restaurant at the intersection of Sanma Road and Zhejiang Road announced that its restaurant, in view of the fact that autumn is approaching and it is appropriate for all walks of life to recuperate, has specially sent commissioners to various places to search for various tonics and seasonal birds and seafood for the enjoyment of all, such as phoenix feet Huaiqi clear stewed deer tendons Huaiqi stewed black chicken phoenix claws soft-shelled turtle heart stewed pigeons, etc. are all seasonal nourishing stews. The original stewed soup is fresh, sweet, and not greasy, which is indeed beneficial to health. Flying birds and seafood such as Wuhua bird, fat Anren braised big fish head, and live black fish are made with novel and delicious flavors that are suitable for the palate. In addition, all kinds of Cantonese-style preserved meats in the preserved meat department have been launched, such as duck liver sausage, duck legs, duck breast, preserved meat, and soy sauce sausage. In recent days, people from all walks of life who have purchased gifts have been quite crowded, it is said.

Huada Pharmacy at the intersection of Fuxu Road and Tongfu Road announced that the Lion Power Beef Juice produced by the German Martha Pharmaceutical Factory, which is managed by the pharmacy, has long been famous all over the world and is recognized by major hospitals and famous doctors in the world. Its effect can increase the essence and strengthen the brain, strengthen the spirit, and produce blood, and is rich in vitamins, proteins, and other vital elements. All those who take it can increase the body's strength and are enough to offset the amount taken by 15 times. Therefore, it is the best tonic for recuperation after illness, and it is suitable for all ages. A large number of new products have been shipped to Xinxin, Wing On, Sincere, major companies, and major pharmacies and food stores.

Huachanglong Shop at Zhongmantingfangkou, Wuma Road, announced that its shop has been established for six years and the speed of business development is rare. The aim is to promote sales with small profits, so it has been praised and favored by all walks of life. Now, we have prepared a large number of domestic silk, satin, woolen cloth, serge, and Guangdong cloth, etc., sacrificing our capital and selling them cheaply to express our sincerity and to celebrate the sixth anniversary. In recent days, purchasers have been extremely crowded, all fearing to miss the good opportunity, it is said.

Shanghai Modern Bookstore announced that the book All Quiet on the Western Front published by the bookstore was originally written by the German Remarque and jointly translated by Mr. Hong Shen and Ma Yanxiang. The book has more than 400 pages and more than 200,000 words, and is accompanied by portraits and biographies of the original author. The original book was published in Germany in January last year, and within three months, there were translations in all countries of the world. The total sales exceeded three million copies, which is a record in the world's literary world. Now, the translation by Hong and Ma is faithful and fluent, and can express the original author's feelings. There is also Ma Yanxiang's nearly 10,000-word preface, which has a very sincere discussion of the value of the book and the difficulty of translation. Hong Shen's postscript has many citations and explanations about war literature. Recently, the Shanghai Nanjing Grand Theater has shown the film All Quiet on the Western Front, which is completely based on Remarque's novel. The general audience who wants to understand the detailed inside story of the film must have one copy per person, and the special price for each copy is one yuan.

Dujinsheng on North Sichuan Road announced that since the factory held a price reduction recently, the retail and wholesale sales have been exceptionally bustling in recent days. The silk landscape and colorful brocades produced by the factory are far from comparable to those produced by other factories. The newly released third edition of art samples is extremely precious, and those who purchase more than ten yuan can receive a copy as a preferential treatment, it is said.

Xinchangmao Hat Store at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Touji Bridge announced that its store specializes in selling various domestic felt hats and high-end European and American felt hats produced by Guanyi Hat Factory. The styles are novel, the prices are low, and the quality is good. Now, the store's renovation has been completed, and the opening ceremony will be held today. All goods will be reduced in price for 21 days, it is said.

Theater News 258

Xindongfang Theater on the north side of Yokohama Bridge, North Sichuan Road, announced that since the theater performed the improved national opera, it has attracted the attention and approval of the community and is indeed a highlight in the theater world. It is heard that the second improved national opera, Three Halls Joint Trial with the Execution Ground, is now being performed. The play is adapted according to the historical biography, and the plot is completely different from the old Jade Hall Spring. The plot is tense and bizarre and requires more than two hours to perform. The scenery is specially made by experts using scientific methods to create more than a dozen three-dimensional scenery, which is completely like the real thing and has never been seen on the Chinese stage today, it is said.

Paris Grand Theater announced that the theater will show Dorothy Gish's masterpiece London A Weak Woman starting today. The film tells the story of a lonely orphan girl who suffers all kinds of hardships and finally ascends from hell to heaven. Gish's performance is gentle, sad, and euphemistic, and her expression is excellent. At the same time, the Russian balalaika king, Bosakov, has also been hired to perform on stage. The tone is melodious and moving, and the fingering is pure, skillful, and agile, which is truly a superb skill, it is said.
